Foreign Important Telegrams

Serious Situation in the Far East: China, Soviet Russia's Promotion of Peace Policies 61

Signing Non-Aggression Pacts with Neighboring Western Countries One After Another

Japan Has No Intention to Conclude a Treaty; Her Militaristic Ambitions are Evident

Romania's Attitude is Solely Dependent on France

Foreign Minister and Prime Minister Have Conflicting Policy Views

Havas News Agency, Moscow, 16th – The Soviet government’s official gazette [Izvestia] stated in today's editorial that the Soviet Union and Romania's negotiations for a mutual non-aggression treaty have been unsuccessful after lengthy talks due to Romania's obstructionist policies, accusing the Romanian government of hindering peace efforts. It is reported that, given the serious situation in the Far East, the Soviet Union is constantly mindful of peace. Therefore, it promotes its peace policies with utmost calm, forcing even the most ardent militarists to temporarily abandon their playful attitude towards peace. The Soviet Union has successively signed non-aggression treaties with Finland, Latvia, Poland, and Estonia. The success of this peace policy is excellent. Even in France, where anti-Soviet forces are rampant, there is a tendency to accept the Soviet Union's peace proposals reluctantly. Romania is the only neighboring country of the Soviet Union that refuses to sign a treaty. Although the Romanian authorities cannot excessively reject the Soviet Union's proposal for a treaty due to the victory of the Soviet Union's peace policy, they have used various excuses to overturn the nearly successful treaty in the past year. Therefore, the Soviet Union is currently awaiting Romania's definitive response: whether it is willing to sign a non-aggression treaty with the Soviet Union like other peace-loving Eastern European countries or to persist in its policy of undermining peace according to the wishes of certain international elements.

TASS News Agency, Moscow, 16th – Today, Soviet newspapers published Foreign Minister Litvinov's remarks on the conclusion of the Russian-Romanian non-aggression treaty. Litvinov first recounted the historical process of the negotiations, pointing out that Romania had twice sent representatives to sign the draft treaty, only to undermine it herself twice. He stated that if Romania genuinely wished to conclude a non-aggression treaty with the Soviet Union and did not intend to achieve other indirect goals through it, the treaty could have been concluded long ago. Litvinov claimed that Romania's inconsistent behavior showed that there must be multiple forces fighting each other within and outside the country, and it was doubtful whether Romania had the sincerity to conclude the treaty, as its responsible representative also stated that such a treaty was not very necessary for Romania. The Romanian representatives often temporarily requested the removal of clauses established after lengthy discussions and replaced them with new clauses, clearly intending to create new disputes, prolong the signing period, or even sabotage the treaty. However, the Soviet Union's sincerity in concluding the treaty has remained consistent. Litvinov considered Romania's proposal to convene countries bordering the Soviet Union to conclude a multilateral treaty useless, believing that the Soviet government wanted to conclude bilateral treaties. As the facts have clearly shown, the Kellogg-Briand Pact was completely powerless to prevent the military conflict between China and Japan, both signatory countries. Therefore, the Soviet Union does not want its solemn treaties with other countries to become the same kind of diplomatic game.

National News Agency, Rome, 15th – Since the return of Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu to the capital, the political situation has not eased its tension, and the rift between Titulescu and Prime Minister Vaida has deepened. Even King Carol's efforts to mediate have had little apparent effect. It is reported that Titulescu still opposes concluding a non-aggression treaty with Soviet Russia, while Vaida insists on continuing direct negotiations with Moscow. Several cabinet members support Titulescu's position, demanding a change in the diplomatic policy that has always followed France's lead. Those close to Titulescu also claim that France recently intends to use League of Nations loans to intensify its control over Romania's diplomacy, making it necessary to plan for self-preservation early.

Havas News Agency, Rome, 16th – Today, during the celebration of the King's birthday, National Peasant Party leader Maniu met with Prime Minister Vaida and Foreign Minister Titulescu. Vaida and Titulescu both completely adhered to their original opinions, so reconciliation between the two seems hopeless. There were previous reports that Interior Minister Mihalache supported Titulescu's views, and there are fears that this would cause a split within the National Peasant Party. This matter seems to have been avoided for the time being, and Vaida's position has been consolidated before the renegotiation of the mutual non-aggression treaty with Soviet Russia. There will be two talks tomorrow, and the King may personally participate in the conclusion. Havas News Agency, Moscow, 16th – TASS News Agency inquired with Foreign Affairs Commissioner Litvinov regarding the Romanian-Soviet negotiations for a mutual non-aggression treaty. Subsequently, the agency received an officially released document describing the course of the negotiations between the two countries. The document mentioned the Riga dispute, stating that a clause was included in the mutual non-aggression treaty declaring that the two countries would not raise various issues of dispute with each other, and the two governments would fully maintain their views on these disputed issues. The Romanian representative firmly opposed including this clause. The official document stated that it is well known that there are disputes between Romania and the Soviet Union, especially the issue of Bessarabia. Moreover, before the start of the negotiations, Romania had already put forward this prerequisite itself. Therefore, there is no legitimate reason for Romania to oppose including this clause. The Romanian side has proposed various forms of non-aggression, but the result of interpreting these plans would be tantamount to the Soviet Union indirectly recognizing the occupation of Bessarabia. Therefore, the Soviet Union clearly rejected these plans and proposed other methods. The method proposed by the Soviet Union clearly indicated that the government allows that disputes would not be resolved by force. This method is tantamount to a complete guarantee to Romania that the Soviet government would not use the Bessarabian issue as an excuse to not abide by the mutual non-aggression treaty. The official document also stated that what the Romanian authorities seek is not to conclude a mutual non-aggression treaty, but to find a way to make the Soviet government indirectly recognize or tacitly approve the occupation of Bessarabia. This can be seen from the discussion.

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 17th – The Russian government has proposed the conclusion of a Japanese-Russian non-aggression treaty as an exchange condition for recognizing "Manchukuo." The Japanese government has not yet taken a clear stance on whether to conclude a non-aggression treaty. However, the great powers are paying close attention to Japanese-Russian relations. The Japanese government has divided opinions on the Japanese-Russian non-aggression treaty, with some arguing that Japan is in a diplomatically isolated position due to the Manchurian problem. Therefore, it should approach Russia and conclude a non-aggression treaty to prevent the intrusion of communist ideology and promote economic cooperation between Japan and Russia. However, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that Japan and Russia are both signatories to the non-war treaty, so there is no need to conclude a non-aggression treaty immediately. Moreover, it believes that those who think that concluding a non-aggression treaty can prevent communist propaganda do not understand the position of the Third International. Therefore, Russia, which is incompatible with Japan's national polity, is a useless associate and must be watched. As for Japan's diplomatic isolation, there is no need to panic, as the countries seem to gradually understand Japan's actions. Therefore, there is no need to change the diplomatic policy, which is a rebuttal to the previous argument.

Japan's Current Politics 63

Reason Cannot Match Emotion

The Military Forces the Finance Minister to Implement Tax Increases

The Saito Cabinet's Crisis Lies in the Budget

Reuters, Tokyo, 17th – The estimated expenses of the budget proposal for the next fiscal year submitted by the various government ministries are said to total 2.4 billion Japanese yen, an increase of approximately 600 million yen compared to the unprecedentedly large budget proposal of 1928-29, and an increase of approximately 800 million yen compared to the average budget proposal of the previous ten years. The Ministry of Finance will, of course, advocate for efforts to economize, but it is believed that the maximum amount that the Ministry of Finance can allow is far from the minimum amount that the ministries deem impossible to reduce, which may cause a serious cabinet crisis. The expenses for the Manchurian war are already huge, and the so-called supplementary expenses of the army and navy are also very large. Therefore, the budget expenses set by the army and navy total more than 1 billion yen. The future dispute will likely lie in these national defense expenses. Although Finance Minister Takahashi has changed Inoue's policy of frugality and not issuing bonds, there is still a shortfall of over 1.3 billion yen in balancing the budget proposal. It is feared that Takahashi may not be able to allow the issuance of this huge debt to make up for it. Moreover, Takahashi is still opposed to increasing direct taxes. It is reported that Army Minister Araki strongly advocates increasing inheritance tax and income tax to raise this amount. If the rumors are true, then the military and Takahashi's supporters will clash greatly. According to many people's speculation, if this happens, the military seems likely to win. As a certain Japanese celebrity stated, in today's Japanese politics, reason often cannot match emotion. If Araki wins, Takahashi will likely be forced to resign, and the cabinet will collapse along with him. The resulting turmoil may be even more serious than after the assassination of Inukai Tsuyoshi.

Japan's Opinions Diverge

The Military Advocates Separate Control of Manchuria

The Colonial Ministry Proposes Joint Control of the Three Colonies

Hua Lian News Agency, Tokyo, 17th – Regarding the issue of economic control between Japan and Manchuria in the Japanese plan, the Japanese government's opinions are divided and still unable to agree. The goal is annexation, but the various parties have slightly different opinions on the method of annexation. The military and the South Manchuria Railway Company argue that the control between Japan and Manchuria should not include Korea, Taiwan, or Karafuto. If they are included together, it would be the same as Korea and Taiwan becoming colonies, making it inconvenient to argue with other countries. This would not only lose the sympathy of other countries, but also be too large in scale and be under the jurisdiction of the Colonial Ministry, preventing the military from obtaining real power. However, the Colonial Ministry advocates that the three colonies of Korea, Taiwan, and Karafuto must be included together to achieve the goal of annexation. If this plan is not accepted by the military, another committee will be organized to control the three colonies, recruiting directors of various ministries and departments, high-ranking colonial officials, and financial magnates as members under the jurisdiction of the Colonial Ministry. Regarding this plan, due to the many divergent opinions from various parties, the final decision will likely be made after the puppet representative Xie Jieshi enters Beijing.

French Senate Re-election 70

Reuters, Paris, 17th – Elections for the French Senate began everywhere today. This is an indirect voting system. Future Tale of Japanese-American Naval War 72

Since the Manchurian and Shanghai incidents, Japan's apprehension towards the United States has increased day by day. On one hand, it seeks to ease international tensions, and on the other, to carry out its policy of aggression in mainland Asia, it is actively preparing for war against Russia and the United States. So-called air defense drills, naval exercises, attempts to smooth things over with various countries, and dispatching representatives are all being arranged with a sense of urgency. In particular, the younger officers in that country, who disregard international public opinion and advocate resolving issues through force, continue to spare no effort. Consequently, in the past few months, no fewer than thirty or forty books regarding [Japanese-American War], [Japanese-Russian War], [War between Japan and England and America], [Future Wars in the Pacific], etc., have been openly published, fully revealing the ambitions of warmongers. The United States, due to various reasons, remains taciturn despite Japan's intimidation. However, the confrontation between the two countries is deepening, and the future eruption of calamity is to be expected. Herewith is a translated summary of the [Future Tale of the Pacific War] as published by the Tokyo Kokumin Shimbun and the [Naval War in the Pacific] as published by the Tokyo Yorozu Choho, to allow readers to understand Japan's preparations for war against the United States. It is not difficult to infer the attitudes that England, Russia, France, Italy, and other countries will adopt after war breaks out between Japan and the United States. – Translator's Note

The Pacific Ocean has never suffered the scourge of war since ancient times. Whether it can maintain its peace in the future is difficult to predict. However, judging from today's international situation, it is feared that it will be difficult to avoid a tragic tragedy. Why is that? Because we (Japan) are being labeled with the ignominious name of aggressor by the United States, and diplomatic relations between the two countries are almost like swords drawn and bows strung, with the potential to explode at any moment. If our country were to go to war with the outside world, it would have to bet its national fortune on coping with them. In addition, our nation's awareness must be prepared for a do-or-die gamble to determine the rise and fall of our national fortune. However, we are confident that the final outcome of this war will not be defeat, because our country's military defense capabilities are already more than sufficient. Although we are not a war-loving people, if we encounter a situation where we want to avoid it but cannot (i.e., when our national policy and diplomatic methods fail to achieve their goals, or when the enthusiasm among the people boils over), then the only final means is to resort to war. If war were to break out, it is feared that more than one country would be our enemy. Japan's military equipment is primarily focused on defense, and a defensive attitude should be adopted to counter enemy countries. Looking at Japan's geography, from the Kuril Islands in the north to Taiwan in the south, with various islands dotted in between, we can draw a battle line and prepare submarines and aircraft to engage in a final decisive battle with the world's powerful nations. This time, unlike the European War, we will not rely entirely on the army as the main force, causing the war to drag on for six or seven years. Because our war with the United States will be a purely naval war, and the outcome of a naval battle can be decided in a short time. The concern is, if war breaks out between Japan and the United States, and England joins the United States against Japan, can Japan's naval battles be victorious? Here is a brief description of the naval strengths of the three countries, England, the United States, and Japan, and the conditions of the Pacific war defenses.

(I) The Existing Strengths of the Three Countries: England, the United States, and Japan. The first requirement for war is the spirit of the people and excellent soldiers. The strength of will to fight and the use of sophisticated weapons are particularly important. Since the Washington and London conferences, Japan's construction of warships has been limited. The naval strengths of England, the United States, and Japan are listed below:

Capital Ships Cruisers Submarines Aircraft Carriers

Japan Ten Thirty-eight Eighty Five

398,084 tons 290,900 tons 80,095 tons 87,000 tons

United States Seventeen Thirty-two One Hundred Twenty-Two Seven

520,038 tons 320,034 tons 120,096 tons

England Eighteen Fifty-three Sixty-four Eight

550,059 tons 337,000 tons 60,012 tons 120,077 tons

(II) The Prediction of War in the Pacific: It is easy to imagine how fierce the war in the Pacific will be. The United States' entire fleet of 1.5 million tons is now concentrated at the San Pedro naval port on the Pacific coast. Its capital ships, such as the West Virginia, are equipped with eight 40cm cannons, and there are also huge coastal guns on the coast, arranged facing west. The aircraft hangars of the Saratoga and Lexington are fully stocked with elite air forces, and everything is presided over by the famous Admiral General Chief of Naval Operations Bullard. As soon as the order is given, they will advance to Hawaii. The Hawaiian Islands are only 3,500 nautical miles from Yokosuka Naval Port. They will use Pearl Harbor as their center and advance westward. At the same time, the fortress of Ma'a Island in the South Pacific and the air force bases in the north, such as Dutch Harbor and other important ports in the Aleutian Islands, will echo each other from afar with the main force in Honolulu, either as their wings or as their waiting ports, operational bases, and supply depots for military supplies. Locations such as San Francisco, Hawaii, the Ogasawara Islands, the Ryukyu Islands, China, and the Philippines must be connected into a line. However, for operational reasons, they will avoid the Ryukyu Islands and the Ogasawara Islands, and focus on Hawaii, Guam, and the Philippines. Guam Island has a strong radio station and is an important relay point for the United States to the Philippines. However, the defense of Guam Island is inferior to that of Hawaii. Yokosuka is 1,000 nautical miles from Guam, and Hawaii is 3,300 nautical miles from Guam. Due to geographical relations, before the arrival of the American fleet, a part of the Japanese fleet can easily capture Guam. Manila in the Philippines is also equipped with fortresses and a standing air force of 1,800 aircraft, including no fewer than 400 fighters, reconnaissance planes, and heavy bombers, as well as one airship. The operational range of its best aircraft is 25,000 kilometers, which will pose a major threat to the skies over the Orient. In peacetime, in order to ensure the safety of commercial routes, the American Oriental Fleet, based in Manila, which is 1,500 nautical miles from Yokosuka, will take a encirclement formation, linking Alaska, the Aleutian Islands, Hawaii, Guam, and the Philippines once war breaks out. May I ask how the defense of the Orient is? Although the Kuril Islands in the north are sufficient to counter Alaska and the Aleutian Islands, and the submarine fleet in the Ogasawara Islands can resist the fleet dispatched from Hawaii, the Ryukyu Islands and the Magong Fortress line in Taiwan in the south are not optimistic for defense naval operations. Moreover, the British Far East Fleet, with the 10,000-ton Kent-class cruiser as its main force, will hold the world's maritime rights with the large fortresses of Hong Kong and Singapore and defend Hong Kong with all its might. On one hand, it will guard the throat between the Orient and India and Europe. The so-called Singapore Fortress and the Australian fleet under its jurisdiction will also participate in the war. Can the Japanese Navy support it at that time? Although our army defeated enemy ships in the Russo-Japanese War, today, with the invention of new weapons and the change of strategy, the air force, which assists naval battles, will be very fierce. How this combat capability will determine the victory or defeat of both sides. According to recent information, the United States has three of the latest aircraft carriers, and Japan has four. Our [Akagi] can compete with the American [Saratoga] and [Lexington]. Comparing their performance, the [Akagi] is 26,900 tons, has a speed of 28 knots, is equipped with 14 high-angle guns and 12 secondary guns, and carries 50 aircraft. The [Saratoga] is 33,000 tons, has a speed of 33 knots, is equipped with 8 primary guns and 12 secondary guns, and carries 83 aircraft. The two ships can bombard each other at a distance of 30,000 meters. However, the Japanese Navy's unique first-class destroyers are the world's unparalleled elite. At present, there are twelve first-class cruisers, such as the large Kako and Furutaka, followed by the Kongo, Hiei, Kirishima, Haruna, Fuso, Yamashiro, Ise, Hyuga, Nagato, and Mutsu battleships, sixty-eight first-class destroyers, and eight that will be completed, including twenty large ones. Considering the combat power, it is not inferior to that of England and the United States.

(III) The Great Naval Battle in the Western Pacific: If Japan and the United States go to war, the American fleet, gathered along the coast of California, will be connected from bow to stern, reaching 250 ships, and will begin to advance westward. They will use the destroyer squadron and patrol ships as the front line, with reconnaissance cruiser squadrons protecting both sides. The flagships West Virginia, Colorado, Maryland, and the 10,000-ton Augusta-class large cruisers, submarine tenders, long-range submarine squadrons, mine warfare squadrons, and other special service ships and super-large aircraft carriers will advance to the base at Pearl Harbor, Hawaii. From Hawaii, they will move westward to meet the enemy. It is expected that the war will be divided into two phases. The first phase of the operation will be the seizure of enemy bases and the active deployment of submarine cruiser squadrons, belonging to a surprise attack. In the battles to capture the two fortresses of Manila and Guam, the war will be very fierce. At that time, Guam, with its relatively inferior defense capabilities, will be occupied by the Japanese army. Manila, with its substantial air force, Far Eastern Fleet, and natural terrain, and equipped with 16-inch cannons, will resist the Japanese army's attack with all its might. However, with Japan's elite fleet, the American Navy will adopt a defensive posture. However, our army, based on the principle of quick battles and quick decisions, will engage in a large battle between the two main fleets. In this way, Manila can be occupied in less than ten days, and then we can advance to the Hawaiian base. Thus, a great naval battle will occur on the western Pacific coast. When our side receives a warning that the American fleet has left Hawaii, the flagship Mutsu, which is waiting in the Ogasawara Islands, 囗囗, 囗囗, etc., will begin to move out. At this time, wooden sailing ships from the Nelson era will be sunk in succession after being shelled by our artillery. After the mine warfare squadron's fierce attack, we will achieve a great victory. (To be continued)

Has telegraphed the military authorities with the inspection results.

Jinan Correspondence: Li Yue and Fan Yuhuang, special commissioners dispatched by the Military and Political Department to inspect Jiaodong, after arriving in Jinan, immediately went to Yexian and Laiyang to conduct inspections. Except for Li Yue, who had already returned to Beijing to report to the Military and Political Department about the meeting with Liu Zhennian's representative, Li Henghua, Fan Yuhuang, who went to Laiyang for inspection, also returned to Jinan by the third Jiaoji train from Jiaoxian at 10:30 last night (the 14th). He stayed at the Jiaoji Hotel. Zhang Shouqian, a senator of the provincial government, also returned to Jinan on the same train as Fan. After resting briefly at the Jiaoji Hotel, Fan went to the Jinan Central Bank to meet Jiang Bocheng to report on the inspection in Laiyang and telegraphed the Military and Political Department and the Military Commission. According to Fan, who spoke to visitors at the Jiaoji Hotel today, the situation in Laiyang is very good. The two sides are more than ten li apart, and the outposts are at Shuigoutou, which is more than fifty li away from Laiyang City. There are many plainclothes troops of Liu's army there, constantly harassing the Third Route Army. The front of the Third Route Army is now the self-defense army organized by the masses in Jiaodong, which often clashes with Liu's plainclothes troops. As for the Third Route Army troops, there have been no clashes with Liu's army. He first went to Gu Xian and then to Shuigoutou, where he stayed for a day. He returned to Pingdu that day and arrived in Jiaoxian from Pingdu the next day. He then returned to Jinan on the third Jiaoji train from Jiaoxian. Whether he goes to Beijing or stays in Jinan will be decided after the military headquarters replies to Jinan by telegram. He has reported the details of his inspection in Laiyang to Chief of General Staff Jiang. The Jiaodong issue will probably be resolved. (October 15th)

Jinan District Court 74

Hearing of Zheng Jicheng's Case

Jinan Correspondence: The provincial government, acting on the order of the Executive Yuan, transferred Zheng Jicheng, the assassin of Zhang Zongchang, who caused a sensation in the north and south, from the Military Law Office of the Third Route Headquarters on the 24th of last month to the Shandong Higher Court. The Higher Court sent it to the Jinan District Court. After repeated interrogations by prosecutors Zhu Weiran and Zhu Fengxiang of the District Prosecutor's Office, Zheng Jicheng was publicly prosecuted on the 7th of this month for the crime of premeditated murder. The detailed circumstances have been described in previous letters. At 9:30 this morning (the 15th), the trial was held publicly in the Criminal Division 1 of the Jinan District Court. The judges Li Hongye, Li Guixin, and Zhou Peiji, the clerk Zhang Piji, the prosecutor Zhu Weiran, the defendant Zheng Jicheng, and Zheng's lawyers Zhou Qingen, Sun Baifu, and Li Yunsheng all arrived on time. Zheng was wearing a gray woolen jacket, blue riding pants, formal woolen multi-layered shoes, with short hair, and looked energetic and smiling. He did not appear tired or exhausted. Bi Shizhen, the patrol chief of the Southwest Township Public Security Bureau, and police officer Cao Yuke, who were present at the time, also testified in court. The gallery was extremely crowded. Hu Xu, the president of the District Court, and most of the court's staff were also present to observe. After the court session began, the judges took their seats and first questioned Zheng Jicheng. They asked Zheng Jicheng's name, age, hometown, occupation, and whether he had committed any crimes before. Zheng replied, "I am Zheng Jicheng, 40 years old, from Licheng, residing at No. 7 Bianzhi Alley. I am currently the director of the Licheng Charity Association and am a person of honor. I have never committed a crime before." They asked how many siblings he had. He replied, "There are four brothers in my branch. My eldest brother has passed away. My second brother and younger brother both work on the Yanwei Road." They asked who Zheng Jinsheng was to him. He replied, "He is my uncle, that is, my adoptive father. I was only a few years old when I was adopted. At that time, my uncle had no children. Later, he had a son in his old age." At this point, the judge asked prosecutor Zhu Weiran what his opinion was on the case. Zhu stood up and said that the main points of his opinion were detailed in the indictment. The judge then asked Zheng Jicheng if he had seen the indictment and if he had anything to say about the prosecutor charging him and Chen Fengshan with conspiring to kill Zhang Zongchang and punishing him according to Article 284 of the Criminal Code, which deals with more serious offenses. Zheng replied, "Killing Zhang Zongchang was to avenge my father's death, and I, as a revolutionary, was removing obstacles for the revolution." They asked if he had shot Liu Huaizhou and Liu Qingxun. He replied, "There were no two Lius when I killed Zhang, and I have never known the two Lius. I have no hatred with them, so how could I kill them?" They asked, "Why did you kill Zhang Zongchang and what were the circumstances at the time?" Zheng replied, "I have already said that killing Zhang Zongchang was to avenge my father, eliminate harm for the people, and remove obstacles for the revolution." They asked, "What day was it?" He replied, "September 3rd." They asked, "Where did you go from?" He replied, "I am the director of the Charity Association. I must go there every lunar 3rd and 6th. It happened to be the 3rd day of the eighth lunar month. I went from home to the association and returned at three o'clock. On the road, I heard people talking about Zhang Zongchang harming Shandong and causing the May 3rd Massacre. It would be better if he died in Shandong to relieve the people's hatred." At that time, I could not help but be moved. When I got home, friends left at one thirty. I ate because I had a stomach illness. Usually, I drink a glass of medicinal wine before meals. After that glass, I thought about the passersby and wanted to kill Zhang. I had a vendetta to avenge my father, so I should kill him even more. At that time, I was on fire and could not eat. I only ate a bowl of rice and told my family that I was going to the train station to send off a friend surnamed Li. I went to Shi You-san's house (Zhang lived in Shi's house) to call and ask if Zhang had left. I didn't get through, so I went to the station with Chen Fengshan by car. When I arrived at the station's west gate cave, Chen Fengshan first shot me and told me that I wanted to kill Zhang to avenge my father and that he was not allowed to fire randomly. I then entered the station, and Chen followed me. When I arrived at the second platform, Zhang Zongchang was already grabbing the car door to see off guests. More than ten people seeing Zhang off under the car were all unfamiliar to me. They all wished Zhang a safe journey. I then took out my gun and shot Zhang. One shot missed. When I was changing the bullet, Zhang shouted "Not good!" and ran into the car. I followed and fired the second shot, which also missed. I changed the bullet again. Zhang ran to the east car door and wanted to get off. I fired the third shot, which still missed. I changed the bullet again. Zhang ran down the car. I chased him down and tripped over iron wire on the second platform. I got up and chased him. When Zhang ran to the north shore of the third platform, I had returned to the south shore and fired the fourth shot, knocking Zhang down under the platform. Because I didn't know if he was dead or not, I went down and shot him in the head twice. Seeing that he was dead, I shouted that I was avenging my father and surrendered to the law enforcement team." They asked, "When was your father, Zheng Jinsheng, killed by Zhang?" He replied, "November 14th, the 16th year." They asked, "How did he die?" He replied, "He was tricked and killed. At that time, my father was the Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Eighth Route Army of the Northern Expedition, and Liu Zhenhua was the Commander-in-Chief, stationed in Caoxian. Division Commander Jiang Mingyu colluded with Zhang and falsely claimed that Zhang wanted to raise the flag of the Blue Sky with a White Sun. My father believed it to be true, was tricked to Jinan, and was brutally murdered. Later, a secret order was issued to arrest me in Tianjin. I escaped to Japan." They asked, "When did you know that Zhang was coming to Jinan?" He replied, "It was on the 2nd of the newspaper. I don't know which day he came. He came and lived in Shi's house. On the morning of the 3rd, I went to the Charity Association at eleven o'clock. I took a car, but the car broke down halfway. I walked back. I didn't bring a gun when I went to the association. I don't remember if Chen Fengshan followed me. I returned to Bianzhi Alley at three o'clock. I don't remember if Chen Fengshan was at my house at that time because I didn't pay attention. I went to the backyard to accompany guests for dinner. If I hadn't heard people say it on the road, I wouldn't have known that Zhang was leaving today. At one o'clock, I called Shi's house, but I didn't get through. I said I was sending a friend surnamed Li to the train, not that Zhang Zongchang's luggage was already on the train. They must have misheard." (To be continued)

Suzhou 76

Detailed Account of the Bizarre Shooting and Tragedy in the West City: No. 30 Fulangzhong Alley in the west city is a well-known institution for manufacturing poison pills. Its scale can be called a giant in Suzhou, and the number of victims is unknown. Unexpectedly, at nine o'clock on the sixteenth night, the sound of knocking on the door was heard from outside. Thinking that the police were coming to search, the person in charge led the others to climb onto the roof and tried to escape to Ye Haimen's house at No. 17 Xiangjiaham. At that time, Ye and his daughter were about to go to bed when they suddenly heard the sound of lead skin on the balcony. They looked through the window and vaguely saw two figures and were greatly frightened. They shouted for catching thieves wildly. The servant Tian San also used a foreign iron dustpan to knock around. Hearing the sound, the neighbors mistakenly thought it was a fire and reported to the West District Fifth Section Fire Brigade by telephone. The firefighters gathered and set off, carrying the fire truck through Tonghefang, Jinjinqiao Alley, and turned to Shengjiaham. At this time, the knockers were scattered at both ends of Fulangzhong Alley and Xiaofennong Alley. The two people on the roof had entered Ye's house and politely asked for help and accommodation. The sound of catching thieves and the sound of fire alarms were rising and chaotic. The firefighters also gathered at the scene, but they did not see any fire. They only heard someone shouting "Fire!" in the crowd and temporarily took refuge in the Sheng's tailor shop in Xiaofennong. Before long, gunshots were heard. The bullets flew from behind, five shots in a row, causing a great tragedy. It was reported that one firefighter from the Fifth Section of the West District, Chen Huasheng, died on the spot, and six people were injured. After the incident, Chief of the Public Security Bureau Mao Naigong, Inspector Zhang Nanchun, Director of the Second Branch Pan Renxian, and the competent officials of the fifth Precinct of the Second Branch, Tour Official Fang Ziqing, guerrillas, county police team, the bandits water police three areas, the detective team and other officials in charge, arrived one after another, inspecting separately. Two half-exploded bullets were found on the wall of No. 19 Shengjiaham at the entrance of Xiaofennong Alley. While they were investigating, a person escaped from the door without a house number between No. 33 and No. 34 Fulangzhong Alley (the side door of the poison pill manufacturing institution) and ran straight to the home of Dr. Gu Yunruo in the opposite Zhaoming Alley. Chief Mao ordered the police to arrest him. He claimed to be named Guo Xianglin. Chief Mao also sent police to search the poison pill institution. Two opium pipes and a large number of poison pills and poison pill seals were confiscated. The seals were printed with the words "Yishang Shanghai Zhongyuan Pharmaceutical Company Sealed". Because there were too many poison pills, police were dispatched to monitor and guard them. Another person named Ye Yi was found upstairs and was taken to the fifth Precinct of the Second Branch together with Guo Xianglin. On the morning of the 17th, they were transferred to the Second Branch and then to the Public Security Bureau. Xu Fu, who was staying at the Guangmin Hospital for treatment, died at 7:30 on the morning of the 17th due to his injuries. The District Court dispatched Prosecutor Qian and coroner to inspect the body at 3:00 p.m. on the same day. The Public Security Bureau is currently investigating the origin of the shooting.

Changshu 77

Major Fire on Xiaodongmen Heng Street: At 7:30 p.m. on the 14th of this month, a fire broke out suddenly at Yixingsheng Paper Store on Heng Street outside Xiaodongmen. Electricity and telephone wires were burned, and the fire was so bright that it was like daylight. The cause of the fire was said to be electrical, or it was said that the store caused the fire by burning paper offerings and accidentally dropped sparks. The streets there were narrow. When the firefighters arrived at the scene, the streets had been burned and they could not get water, which caused the fire to spread to the neighbors on the left and right and also to the Huayuanham shops in Nanmen. Fortunately, the Central District Fire Brigade detoured to Huayuanham to put out the fire, and it gradually subsided. It is reported that the burned shops were: Miaoxingsheng Fish Shop, Yixingsheng Paper Store, Sanshanzhen Meat Shop, Tongsheng Native Goods Shop, Donglai Candle Shop, Shi Yongtai Silver Shop, Wanmaotong Oil Shop, Hongmao Hotel on Heng Street, and Yangshunxing Water Mill Shop and Zhang Tongxing Fresh Meat Shop on Huayuanham. Other shops, such as Hexing Wine Shop, Lu Gongji Fish Shop, and Shenyu Cigarette Shop, were spared from being burned because firefighters tore down those shops. Among them, only Tongsheng and Yixingsheng Paper Store had fire insurance, and the rest had no compensation at all. It is estimated that more than twenty houses were destroyed, about one hundred and several rooms, and the loss was about 200,000 gold. Tongsheng's loss was the greatest. Wang Genda, the owner of Yixingsheng store, was ill in bed. The fire burned the mosquito net before he escaped naked, and the skin on his lower body was burned. His wife was also slightly injured. He was sent to the hospital for treatment. It is said that Wang's life is worrying, and one of the firefighters fell from the roof and was seriously injured.

Wuxi 78

All Silk Factories Resumed Work Yesterday

The general strike of silk factories throughout Wuxi County has now come to an end. All factories resumed work uniformly today (the 17th). Yesterday afternoon, the three provincial committee members, He Yushu, Li Mingyang, and Zhang Gongren, convened a meeting with labor representatives at the Railway Hotel. Approximately forty people attended, including the nine executive committee members of the Silk Factory Industry Association, one male and one female worker representative each, and representatives from various factories. County Magistrate Chen also attended. First, County Magistrate Chen explained the purpose of the meeting. Following him, the three provincial committee members, He, Li, and Zhang, gave instructions successively. The main idea was that silk is China's only major export commodity. Recently, due to the dumping of Japanese silk abroad, the market has been heavily pressured, leading to a downturn. During this time of national crisis, it is imperative to strive for unity between labor and capital to revive the silk market and resist the Japanese encroachment and dumping, which is already a challenge. Now, a labor strike has occurred, and the dispute remains unresolved. This is tantamount to pushing the silk industry into a dead end and giving the Japanese an opportunity to develop. Therefore, the provincial government is deeply distressed and attaches great importance to this issue, so we were dispatched to mediate. The provincial government's main focus for resolving this labor dispute is to resume work first and then mediate. If anyone deliberately disobeys or stirs up trouble, they will be dealt with according to military law. Regarding the labor's demands, we will, within a possible range, take into account the interests of both labor and capital and arbitrate fairly. If there is indeed undue oppression by the capital side that the labor cannot tolerate, the capital side will be strictly ordered to improve. However, the fact that the silk market is depressed and that the factories are on the verge of collapse must also be taken into account at the same time, and so on. The meeting adjourned at around 3 p.m., and then a meeting was convened with the capital side. At 6:30 p.m., He, Li, and Zhang reconvened the military and police to discuss matters such as protecting the resumption of work and organizing patrol teams to set out on patrols. That evening, the three committee members, He, Li, and Zhang, immediately summoned both labor and capital to discuss the fair compromise, telegraphed the county government for instructions, and sent a letter to the county party headquarters ordering the announcement to both parties for their information. Any actions that disrupt public order are strictly prohibited. The compromise stipulated: 1. Working hours: Work begins at 5:45 a.m. and ends at 6:15 p.m. daily. 2. Bonuses: For those who work a full ten days each month, a bonus of one day's work is awarded. For those who work a full sixteen days, a bonus of two days' work is awarded. If work is stopped for half a day, half a day's work is deducted. If work is stopped for one day, one day's work is deducted, and so on. 3. Wages: A. For those on a monthly salary system: 43 cents. B. For those on a point system: The minimum wage shall not be less than 33 cents. 4. All factories must comply with the above three items without exception. 5. For the time being, the above-mentioned method will be implemented. During the effective period of the agreement, if the price of mid-grade silk rises to 850 taels, the original agreement should be restored. At the same time, all executive committee members of the Silk Factory Industry Association immediately notified all workers of the above-mentioned method, instructing them to work with peace of mind and strictly observe order. This morning at 4:30 a.m., the executive committee members set out separately to persuade and guide the female workers to work. The three committee members, He, Li, and Zhang, considering that the labor strike had been settled and their mission had been completed, planned to visit the People's Education Institute today, attend the County Chamber of Commerce's meeting on people's food, and then leave Wuxi to return to their towns.

Nantong 79

Communists Arrested in Tong, Rugao, and Hai Counties, to be Sent to the Provincial Government

The provincial government, noting that many communist suspects have been arrested in Nantong, Rugao, and Haimen counties, has specifically ordered the county magistrates to promptly send all suspects to the Provisional Military Tribunal of the provincial government for trial.

Yangzhou 80

Ancient Artifacts Discovered Due to Riverbank Collapse

Nijia Bridge in the eastern countryside of Yangzhou County is located along the Yangtze River. Since the floods occurred last year, collapses and landslides have been frequently observed, especially recently. Local residents are startled several times a night and have moved away in groups. Several days ago, another collapse occurred with a loud crash, submerging dozens of acres. In the sunken area, an ancient coffin was discovered. A resident, Huang, gathered people to exhume the bones. While opening the coffin, five ancient bricks were unearthed from the loess pile. On the left side was the inscription "Yongchang, Year Nine." On the upper right corner were the two characters "Wang Shi" in ancient seal script. Although eroded and damaged, they were still recognizable. According to historical records, Yongchang was the reign title of Emperor Yuan of Jin. These bricks must be from the Jin Dynasty. After obtaining the bricks, Huang ordered further digging into the spring, where dozens of ancient copper coins were found with strange and profound inscriptions, making it impossible to identify the dynasty to which they belonged. Also found were jade figures, bracelets, mud bricks, and earthen jars, all with extremely ancient and rich colors, which are delightful.

Reduction or Exemption of Grain Tax in Western Farmlands

The crops in the western mountainous areas of this county have been sparse since the summer due to scarce rainfall, and the ditches and ponds are dried up, making irrigation impossible, resulting in withering and barrenness. The villagers have reported the disaster one after another. Previously, County Magistrate Yang, accompanied by Tao Zeji, the director of the first section of the Finance Bureau, went to the 9th and 10th districts to conduct on-site inspections. The areas most severely affected are the eight villages of Chenjiaji, Xiejiaji, Yijuji, Liujiaji, Ganquanshan, Dingguji, Dayiji, and Hangjiaji in the 9th district, and the two villages of Leitang and Beishanying in the 10th district. The three villages of Gongdaoqiao Yangshou, Fangjiaji, etc. in the 9th district, and the eight villages of Yugaotang Bridge, Da Hao Village, Da Yi Village, Liangjiaxiang, Nianqiao Village, Huangjue Bridge, Northern Temple, Kongjia Bridge etc. in the 10th district are less affected. It has now been stipulated that the affected paddy fields in these two districts will have a reduction of 65% in the silver and rice tax, while the mountain paddy fields will have a reduction of 70% in the silver and rice tax, and the mountain fields will be completely exempt. Although the autumn crops in the remaining districts 2, 4, 7, and 8 have been bountiful, many farmers did not plant wheat due to the previous year's flood, and the villagers requested exemption from upper rush work. County Magistrate Yang has now decided to combine this with the autumn survey according to the disaster survey regulations, and during the lower rush work, the silver and rice tax to be paid will be reduced by 60% out of 100%, and the reed tax will be treated the same. According to statistics, the reduction percentage for the transport rice fields is 22% out of 100%, and the reed tax is 6% out of 100%. As for the military colonies of Yangzhou and Zhenjiang, most of the fields are scattered everywhere and the soil is barren. Only after careful consideration, the military colonies in Yangzhou and Zhenjiang will have a general reduction of 25% in Jiangdu, a general reduction of 70% in Ganquan, and the Zhenjiang military colonies will have a general reduction of 30% in Jiangdu. A comparative table has been drafted and submitted to the three departments of the Provincial Government, Civil Affairs, Finance, and Industry, for review and approval.

Bandit Leader Xu Zhiqing Executed by Firing Squad

Xu Zhiqing, a bandit from southern Luhe who engaged in kidnapping for ransom, had long been wanted by the county government. He was recently captured by the Capital Garrison Headquarters. After receiving the news, County Magistrate Chen sent a letter to the headquarters to bring the suspect to Luhe for interrogation. A telegram was received from the provincial government a few days ago, approving the execution. After receiving the telegram, County Magistrate Chen, on the afternoon of yesterday (the 15th), identified the suspect, verified his identity, and escorted him to the execution ground to be executed by firing squad.

(Education News) (Featured)

A Humble Proposal for Reforming Chinese School Education 82

(9) Cheng Tianfang

Vocational schools should enroll high school graduates who cannot enter universities and provide them with specialized skills training to make them highly productive individuals. Because they require more complete equipment, each school can only focus on one subject, such as agriculture, industry, or medicine. However, each subject should be divided into classes according to the needs of society. The curriculum and duration of study for each class can be determined according to the nature of the profession and the interests of the students. For example, an industrial vocational school can be divided into civil engineering, chemical engineering, etc. However, even if they are studying the same civil engineering, if A has higher aptitude and his economic situation allows him to receive longer training, then he can study for four years and graduate as a junior engineer or engineer assistant. If B has lower aptitude and his family does not allow him to study for a long time, he can enter a two-year graduation class and graduate as an engineer assistant or foreman. Although they are in the same school and graduate in the same subject, the length of study can be different. As long as the certificate specifies the duration of study and the subjects studied, society will naturally be able to distinguish their levels and there will be no mistakes. The same applies to other engineering fields, as well as agriculture, commerce, and medicine.

The nature of vocational schools is the same as that of ordinary vocational schools, and they should absolutely focus on production skills. Agricultural schools must be integrated with farms, industrial schools must be integrated with factories, commercial schools must be integrated with stores, and medical schools must be integrated with hospitals and pharmacies. Many courses should be studied on farms, in factories, and in hospitals and pharmacies, rather than in classrooms. In other words, practical education must replace textbook education. Only then can vocational school students truly be able to engage in the production business of the subject they studied after graduation. According to the Ministry of Education's Higher Education Statistics for the 19th year of the Republic of China, there are 27 specialized schools in the country, including 21 public and 6 private. Apart from law, politics, art, music, salt administration, police, taxation, and Sinology, there are 13 others that have a production education nature equivalent to what we call vocational schools, including 4 in industry, 3 each in agriculture and medicine, 1 in fisheries, 1 in commerce, and 1 in merchant marine. These 13 schools have a total of only 1,244 students. Judging from this number, it is far from enough to meet the needs of the country. However, most of the two or three hundred students who graduate each year are anxiously looking for work in society all day long. On the one hand, it is because society is unstable and various businesses are not developing. On the other hand, it is because most vocational school students still receive an education that emphasizes textbooks rather than practice, and they cannot produce after graduation. This is the point that should be paid the most attention to in reforming vocational schools.

The government should formulate a comprehensive plan for vocational schools. First, it should clearly see which province needs which type of people, and then train that type of people. There is no need to train people who are not needed, and the people who are trained must meet the needs of society. For example, the provinces south of the Yangtze River are currently building highways on a large scale, so specialized vocational schools should be established to train highway engineers. The Huai River Basin is vigorously developing water conservancy, so specialized schools should be established to train water conservancy engineers. By analogy, places that produce porcelain should run porcelain schools to study and improve porcelain, and places that produce paper can run paper schools to study and improve paper. The more vocational schools there are that can meet the needs of society, the better.

Now, let's talk about universities. Apart from normal universities and political science universities, which should be established separately, the rest can be established jointly or separately. Those that are established jointly are called universities, and they are divided into arts, sciences, engineering, agriculture, etc. Those that are established separately are called colleges, such as the College of Arts, the College of Science, and the College of Engineering. The nature of universities is fundamentally different from the nature of vocational schools. Vocational schools focus on skills training, while universities should focus on the exploration of academic theories and the research of problems. Only a few people in any country can do this kind of work, and only a few people need to do it. Therefore, vocational schools can be established in large numbers, while universities absolutely emphasize quality over quantity and do not need to be established in large numbers. A well-equipped university that is run conscientiously and can truly cultivate talent is better than ten simple, superficial, and unworthy universities. A university graduate who is willing to think, willing to research, and able to lead society forward is better than fifty university graduates who have no expertise, no ability, cannot use their thinking, and cannot lead society. Therefore, apart from the United States, even in countries with extremely high levels of education, such as England and Germany, the number of universities in the country is very, very small. However, these few universities are where the country concentrates its efforts, so all academic talents and business talents can be cultivated there. If we include both colleges and universities in the United States, there are more than 800, which is a shocking number. However, strictly speaking, among these 800 universities, the number that are truly well-run and worthy of being called universities is probably no more than 30. The rest can only be regarded as vocational schools. Many scholars in the United States are deeply dissatisfied with the abuse of the name of universities in their own country. For example, Abraham Flexner in his book "Universities: American, English, German" frankly criticized the shortcomings of American universities. Not only did he attack the general universities that are just filling numbers, but he also pointed out many problems with even very famous universities, such as Chicago and Columbia.

Unfortunately, in recent years, China has imitated the United States in many things. As a result, the American idea that universities are valued for their quantity has unconsciously penetrated the minds of Chinese people. Therefore, the country has added universities, the localities have added universities, and private individuals have added universities. Universities are established in the east and universities are established in the west. During the peak period of universities, there were nearly 30 universities in Shanghai alone. Newspapers were full of advertisements for university enrollment, which was a grand sight. If we only pursue the name without pursuing the reality, then the level of education in Shanghai can truly be ranked first in the world. Some people in this use the pretext of running a university to raise money, and these people are undoubtedly conscience-stricken and guilty of unforgivable crimes. However, there are also some people who are indeed taking out money to run universities, and this is because they have fallen into the trap of "universities are valued for their quantity." Although American universities are rampant, at least they still have considerable equipment and are at least running them seriously. Therefore, many schools, although they should not be called universities, are at least still vocational schools, and the students who graduate from them can still find considerable jobs. As for China, as long as you rent a few foreign houses, hire a few teachers, and recruit a few students, regardless of whether there are books and instruments, and regardless of the level of students, you can hang up a signboard and immediately become an institution of higher learning. People who graduate from this kind of institution of higher learning are not only not worthy of being called talents, but they also lack ordinary knowledge and skills. They naturally become high-level idlers in society, causing various social unrest phenomena, harming individuals on the one hand and harming the country and society on the other.

Zhejiang Education Department Prepares for High School Graduation Examinations 84

Collection of Examination Questions

No High School Graduating Classes This Semester

More Than Twenty Junior High School Graduating Classes

In the second semester of the previous year, the Zhejiang Education Department received the "Provisional Regulations for Graduation Examinations for Elementary and Secondary School Students" promulgated by the Ministry of Education. Except for elementary school graduates, who have had graduation examinations in various counties and cities, and were ordered to comply with the Ministry's order, the high school graduation examinations were to be held for the first time. Due to insufficient preparation, it was proposed to postpone them to this semester. It has been reported to the Ministry of Education and approved. It is now heard that the Education Department has found that there are no high school graduating classes in the various middle schools in the province this semester. There are only more than twenty junior high school graduating classes. It is urgent to hold the examinations in accordance with the regulations. Preparations for the examinations are currently being actively made. The organizational regulations of the committee, the detailed rules of education, the examination methods, and the methods of calculating scores have been drafted and submitted to the Ministry of Education for review. In order to ensure that the examination questions are suitable for the actual teaching situation in various schools and that the graduating students of various schools can practice in advance, the "Measures for Collecting Examination Questions for the Spring Junior High School Graduation Examinations of the 21st Year" have been formulated and issued to the middle schools throughout the province for compliance by the end of this month. The attached measures are as follows:

(1) In order to ensure that the examination questions are suitable for the actual teaching situation in various schools and that the graduating students of various schools can practice in advance, the department has formulated the "Measures for Collecting Examination Questions for the Spring Junior High School Graduation Examinations of the 21st Year" and issued them to the middle schools throughout the province for compliance. (2) After receiving the order, each school should immediately have each teacher formulate examination questions for each subject of the examination separately, and the school should submit them to the department before October 31 for reference by the department's examination committee. (3) Each school can guide the trial of the self-formulated examination questions for each subject in the school's graduating class to practice. (4) The examination questions for each subject are not limited to the teaching materials of the last semester, but should be based on all the teaching materials of the three years, and the allocation should be made in a comprehensive manner without adding emphasis. (5) The examination questions for each subject are not limited to the textbooks used by the school, but should be based on a mixture of the current textbooks in the market. (6) The scope of the examination questions for each subject is based on the "Provisional Curriculum Standards" promulgated by the Ministry. (7) Except for Chinese and foreign languages, which can have various types of essay questions, and mathematics, which can have ordinary question types, the examination questions for each subject should all use test question types. The number of test questions is not limited, but various test question types, such as true or false, multiple choice, and fill-in-the-blank, should be used. (8) The test content is not limited to factual memory, and all understanding and reasoning, etc., can be tested. (9) The examination questions should be attached with answers, and the answers to the examination questions should avoid being cumbersome and strive for accuracy. (10) Physical education is temporarily examined by each original school in accordance with the Ministry of Education's interpretation, and the scores are sent to the department for review, and there is no need to formulate examination questions. When necessary, the drawing of examination questions will be stipulated separately.

Orders All Counties to Promote Uniformly

Since the former Director of the Education Department, Cheng, appointed Xu Zejun to return to his hometown to head education in Xuyi, he has worked hard to reorganize it. However, due to rampant bandits, combined with floods and droughts, the economy is in a state of collapse. Director Xu has strived to support it and has not stopped teaching. Li Zuwei Receives a Doctorate in Medicine 90

Mr. Li Zuwei is from Putian County, Fujian Province. He graduated from Chiba Medical University in Japan in the 16th year of the Republic of China and immediately entered the research department, specializing in surgery. During the five years, he published many valuable achievements and was highly respected by the surgical community in Japan. When he returned to China in the autumn of last year, he submitted a doctoral dissertation to the university, (1) Experimental study on pancreatic anastomosis and reference papers (2) Demonstration of fat cells in gastric juice: The value of early diagnosis of gastric cancer (3) Surgical complications of enteric fever (4) Surgical significance of brewer's yeast. The professor committee has reviewed and approved it and awarded him a doctorate in medicine. He is truly a rare talent in our country's surgical community. He currently serves as the dean of the Southeast Medical College in Shanghai and the director of surgery at the Southeast Hospital. Mr. Li not only has a profound research on surgery, but also has unique insights on surgery.

New Basketball Techniques (13) (Not Allowed) Original by Claire Burcky (Reprinted) Translated Jointly by Zhang Guodong and Qian Yiqin. Whenever a ball is thrown out of bounds near the basket, the attacking team can easily gain possession. Therefore, the defending team must be especially vigilant. Without skillful throwing and passing, good opportunities are often missed, leading to regret. Now, the American basketball coach Ward Lambert has used the quick advance and straight-throw shot method to instruct the Purdue Team, and it has been very effective. Now, the diagram is recorded as follows:

Number 1 holds the ball and stands outside the baseline under the basket. Numbers 2 and 4 stand on either side of the free throw circle, facing the basket. Number 3 stands about one yard behind the center of the two. Then, Numbers 2 and 4 run towards the corners to lure away their defenders. At the same time, Number 3 runs forward to receive the pass from Number 1 and shoot.

Random Jottings

Bottle Appraisal 120

— Zhan Lu

Two colleagues, Mr. A and Mr. B, each bought a thermos from the market: the brand was the same, the price was the same, the capacity was the same, and the 24-hour insulation claim was also the same. They thought these two thermoses were identical in every way.

Who knew, it wasn't so. After the specified 24 hours, they each tested their own thermos, and the results were very different. The water in Mr. A's thermos was still steaming, while the water in Mr. B's thermos was almost as cold as water.

The result of this test naturally attracted the attention of Mr. A and Mr. B. At first, they thought it was just that one thermos was good and the other was bad, one conducting heat and the other not. Later, after repeated discussions, they found an answer: both Mr. A and Mr. B's thermoses did not conduct heat, Mr. A did not open the thermos's mouth within 24 hours, so it retained the heat inside. Mr. B was eager to know the temperature of the water in the thermos, and had opened the thermos's mouth eight or nine times within 24 hours, so it's no wonder that the heat inside gradually dissipated.

Mr. × sighed and said from the side:

Treat all catchphrases like this.

Mr. A and Mr. B asked the reason, Mr. × said:

Long-term resistance, not losing an inch of land, is a catchphrase in the political world.

A patriotic heart, not daring to fall behind, henceforth not buying enemy goods, is a catchphrase in the business world.

Sleeping on brushwood and tasting gall, returning my rivers and mountains, focusing on military training, vowing to avenge the country's shame, is a catchphrase in the academic world.

Pillowing on spears and awaiting orders, acting swiftly, any sacrifice, vowing not to submit, is a catchphrase in the military world hiding within the passes.

Opening your mouth once reduces the heat by one point; treat all catchphrases like this.

Political world, business world, academic world, and the military world hiding within the passes, I advise you to preserve the temperature in your thermos, do not open the thermos mouth frequently, turning the hot water inside into cold water.

Hope 121

— Qi Wo

丨Enough is Enough丨

Hope is a harlot, she is indulgent and passionate. Her beautiful face attracts the love and admiration of countless people. Her alluring smile bewitches the crazy worshippers around her. She uses her innate magic to control everyone's heart, making everyone willing to devote all their energy to her, even throwing away their precious lives. However, she is not a woman faithful to love after all. She has no chastity, no fixed rationality, no pure love. Her deceptive tricks are very clever, and no man who chases her can obtain final satisfaction.

After I turned a foreign writer's clever metaphor into the paragraph above, I feel that the writer's words are ultimately profound and widely applicable, and in today's China, can't we find countless examples? But at the same time, I also feel that hope's ability to guide people upwards is always indelible. Who doesn't have hope? What career success has not been encouraged by hope? However, in China, which is addicted to hope, hope has truly become a dangerous harlot.

Obviously, the entire Chinese nation is now immersed in a dream-like life of hope. The government authorities hope that the League of Nations will uphold justice, hope that the United States will maintain the dignity of the Nine-Power Treaty, and hope that the Shenyang Incident will have the same outcome as the Jinan Incident. Ordinary people hope that Japan will [collapse on its own,] hope for a Japanese-American war, a Japanese-Russian war, hope that a true Son of Heaven will be born, hope that a sword immortal or flying general will descend from the sky and kill hundreds of thousands of Japanese soldiers. In short, there is no longer any element of self-awareness and self-confidence in the national consciousness. Fated thoughts have occupied this large nation. Everyone lacks a positive understanding of the facts. When we saw the best-selling of books like Tui Bei Tu and Shao Bing Ge during the Shanghai war, we can know how our nation's life is trapped in the circle of hope.

Indulging in hope leads to fantasy and unwillingness to think of practical solutions. Even if there are solutions, there is a lack of strong will to implement them. This is a sign of the nation's lack of self-confidence. This is a symbol of the nation's morbid state. This alone is enough to destroy China. Therefore, I believe that China's danger lies not in the current national crisis, but in the deformed national morbid life. I hope everyone can remember the words of this foreign writer, and all difficulties can naturally be eliminated under a firm and resolute spirit.

Before······Now 122

— Yu Jianhua

丨Let's Compare丨

(1) Before, parents forced their children to marry; now, children force their parents to marry (nowadays, cohabitation after falling in love is prevalent, often with prior relations, and a superficial wedding ceremony is only held when the woman is heavily pregnant).

(2) Before, the poorer people were, the more they could study; now, the poorer people are, the less they can study (schools have become shops, specializing in selling decorations for the children of the bourgeoisie, and the tuition is so high that poor people are speechless).

(3) Before, tailors were slaves to clothes; now, people who wear clothes are slaves to tailors (because of custom-made fashion, tailors, if they can innovate patterns, will not worry about fashionable ladies coming to patronize them).

(4) Before, female students made it their business to eliminate decorations; now, female students make it their business to study decorations.

(5) Before, people controlled houses; now, houses control people (rent is too expensive, so we have to make do).

(6) Before, electricity was more expensive than water; now, water is more expensive than electricity (since setting up our own water meter, the price of water has even exceeded the rent).

National Exhibition Anecdotes 123

— Li Qun

丨Labor-Capital Cooperation Increases Production丨

The National Products Exhibition in this city has been open for several days at the Penglai Market in Nanshi. Its publicity methods, as well as the post office's stamping of the [Encourage the Use of National Products] stamp on letters, are all very enthusiastic, enough to awaken the deaf and inspire people. Here are some of my observations from the exhibition:

On the opening day, the number of guests and visitors from all walks of life reached more than 10,000. In the days that followed, it was still crowded. It is estimated that more than 200 manufacturers participated, displaying more than 4,000 commodities, a dazzling array of beautiful things. Among them, there are many kinds of goods that are equal to foreign goods in terms of quality and price, showing the rapid development of national industry in recent years, and proving that the Chinese people have long paid close attention to local products. Most of the goods listed in the exhibition were daily necessities, followed by food and beverages, and then educational supplies, all of which were able to compete with foreign goods. However, many important imported goods, such as newsprint, rayon, thin paper used for printing, dry plates used for photography, and utensils, were missing from domestic products. Chemical products, scientific instruments, high-quality woolen fabrics, etc., were also not common. This is partly because our country's scientific level is still difficult to catch up with advanced countries, and partly because the domestic situation has been turbulent, disasters have spread everywhere, the economy has been exhausted, funds have been difficult, and labor-capital disputes have frequently occurred in various factories, resulting in national industry facing thorns. It is hoped that our country's entrepreneurs, capitalists, and the labor world will work hard in this difficult time: not to be discouraged by the dangerous environment, but to eliminate prejudices and strive for cooperation. As for the government, it should fulfill its responsibility to protect and encourage new industries, so that the future of national products may be bright and splendid!

The exhibition hall is divided into two parts, north and south. The one located in the north is the first exhibition hall, and the one located in the south is the second exhibition hall. Various national products are mostly placed in glass cabinets, in an orderly manner. Moreover, the arrangement is winding and winding, which contains a lot of beautification, so that the audience has the opportunity to appreciate each item. In the second exhibition hall, the most eye-catching and amazing thing for the audience is the Lighthouse brand foam fire extinguisher produced by the Xin Guang Chemical Industry Company. This machine is divided into four types: fire-fighting type, standard type, boat and car type, and portable type, all of which are made of thin steel plate, and the compound is applied in the middle to ensure that the medicine and the machine do not have chemical reactions. The exterior is also coated with new-style paint and equipped with chromium covers, which are bright and eye-catching. A few weeks ago, it was publicly performed in Nanshi and was praised by various fire brigades and audiences. This is enough to add a different color to the national product world.

It is said that Mr. Zhang Qiuchong, the editor of the short-message magazine Wansui, readers say that he can get the true meaning of the three words [True] [Beauty] [Good]. The sixth issue has been published on the 16th. In addition to the five long articles by Haiming, Chunfan, Xunzi, Zhuo Dai, and Qiuchong, and the continuous [Two Sisters], [Evolution of Shanghai Brothels], [Nonsense], and [Shanghai in the Last Ten Years] and other famous works, there are more than ten masterpieces by Xiaodie, Ban Kuang, and Yiyun, which are exceptionally valuable. It is heard that the company is continuing to solicit 10,000 subscribers to commemorate the expansion, and subscribing to the whole year before the end of the month will only cost five yuan.

Postal Companions into the Pass (15) 124

— Seeking Happiness Studio Owner

On the night of September 18th, the entire city of Shenyang, ×yang City, was easily occupied by the Japanese army. The family heard that Japanese soldiers were killing Chinese people on the streets and alleys outside with guns and bayonets, so they closed the doors tightly, and no one dared to go out. Tong Yizhen's uncle could no longer look for Deputy Commander Gao and Commander Li to scout out how the conspiracy to harm his niece was going to be carried out. As for these two commanders and one deputy commander, two dignified Chinese military men, they were extremely well-informed about important news concerning their lives. They had already heard that the Japanese were going to severely punish the old regime and would not allow them to live in power again, so they quickly took to their heels and abandoned some of the ready-made property in the official residence, took off the tiger-skin military uniform, and disguised themselves as miserable coolies. They dared not take cars anymore, so they walked to Huanggu Village, took a third-class car on the Beining Railway, and hid inside Shanhaiguan with the general refugees. Anyway, they could still live a carefree life in Tianjin, and there might even be better women to play with. There was no need to stubbornly occupy Tong's female student as their fifth concubine, and they easily and easily forgot about Tong Yizhen, just as they forgot about their ancestors' tombs, mulberry and elm home in the three northeastern provinces.

This was to Tong Yizhen's advantage, and she was able to turn danger into safety and eliminate the imminent disaster. Moreover, through this difficult and solid union, she and Lu Boqin measured the true height of each other's love, and the height of their love also increased to the boiling point, becoming even more harmonious than before.

It's just that the current situation is too pessimistic, and their environment is still depressing and bad. Since the Japanese army occupied Shenyang and other parts of the Northeast, it has created a very terrifying world. Residents flocked to the pass, and almost nine out of ten well-off families moved away. Those who were burdened by poverty and could not move could only close their doors and sit at home trembling and waiting for death. They no longer dared to walk on the streets. The park outside Xiaoxibianmen was full of Japanese soldiers, and the Wanquan River seemed to be separated by a planet. There were checkpoints along the way, and the corpses of those killed by Japanese soldiers' guns and bayonets were piled up, so no one dared to risk going there to visit. At this time, it was difficult for this pair of lovers to continue to seek a place to meet in the morning and evening. They had no good place to go, so they had to continue to make secret appointments and still hold a hasty open-air meeting in a quiet place in the lane. Although Tong's uncle and aunt no longer hindered Yizhen's freedom of action, they only urged her out of kindness not to run around and cause trouble.
