Provisional Municipal Council 125

Councilors Inaugurated Yesterday

Chu Minyi Represents the Central Government to Supervise the Oath

First Consultation Meeting Held Immediately

Previously, the Municipal Government, in accordance with the provisions of the Municipal Organization Law, should have established a Municipal Council. However, the autonomous elections were still in progress, and all of the city's reconstruction projects urgently needed to be carried out. The public opinion organ was extremely urgent. Therefore, Mayor Wu and Central Committee Member Chu Minyi jointly proposed to the Central Standing Committee to establish a Provisional Municipal Council to meet the current needs, which was subsequently approved. Organizational regulations were promulgated, and the mayor recommended to the Executive Yuan to appoint Yu Qiaqing and nineteen others as councilors. These matters have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. Now, the Provisional Municipal Council was officially established yesterday morning at the Foreign Affairs Building in Fenglin Bridge. The grand occasion of its establishment ceremony is recorded as follows:

Venue Arrangement: The Foreign Affairs Building was specially decorated with two arches of pine and cypress and colored decorations, erected high at the outer entrance and the main entrance of the office. Two plaques were hung horizontally, adorned with phrases,

one saying [Spirit of Democracy] and the other saying [Promote Public Opinion]. At the entrance of the office, signing tables were set up on both sides. The room on the left was for receiving guests. Upstairs was the grand auditorium, with a portrait of Sun Yat-sen hanging in the middle, with the Kuomintang and national flags crossed on either side. On both sides of the podium were Chinese and Western recording desks. More than two hundred seats were arranged in a circular shape. The seats on the left were for the councilors, and the seats on the right were for guests from the municipal government and various agencies. The remaining seats were for guests. The venue was decorated with balloons, creating a very solemn and beautiful atmosphere. When the guests arrived, Mayor Wu Tiecheng led the municipal government staff to warmly receive them. The Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched police to maintain order at the venue. The Municipal Public Security Bureau music band played music at the venue.

Guests Attending: Yesterday morning at nine o'clock, in front of the Foreign Affairs Building in Fenglin Bridge, there was heavy traffic. Guests and councilors arrived one after another. Among them were Central Committee Member Chu Minyi, the oath supervisor sent by the Central Government and the Executive Yuan; Pan Gongzhan, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters; representatives from the Garrison Headquarters, Jianghai Customs, the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Second Special District Local Court, the China Merchants Bureau Supervisory Office, the Bank Association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, and the Municipal Guoshu (National Martial Arts) Museum; and Mayor Wu of the Municipal Government, Secretary-General Yu, heads of various bureaus, various staff members, and chiefs of various districts of the Public Security Bureau, totaling no fewer than four or five hundred people.

Councilors Attending: Fourteen councilors attended, including Wang Yiting, Shi Zuicai, Du Yuesheng, Wu Jingxiong, Wu Yugan, Chen Guangfu, Qin Runqing, and Liu Zhanen. Five councilors were absent: Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, Li Ming, Chen Bingqian, and Qian Xinzhi. Li Ming went to Nanyang on business, Qian Xinzhi was ill, and Chen Bingqian was busy with affairs. Wang Xiaolai and Wang Yansong were summoned to Wuhan by Generalissimo Chiang Kai-shek. Yesterday, the two sent a telegram to the council, requesting Yu Qiaqing and Qin Runqing to represent them. The telegram read: "To the Shanghai Municipal Government, transferred to the gentlemen of the Municipal Council, Xiaolai was summoned to Hankou and has not been able to fly back to attend the council inauguration. Please Elder Yu Qiao represent. Please Brother Qin Runqing represent. Xiaolai and Song respectfully kowtow."

Proceedings of the Meeting: At ten o'clock in the morning, the meeting was convened with the ringing of a bell. First, the Municipal Council elected Yu Qiaqing as the temporary chairman. The ceremony was as follows: (1) Music; (2) Chairman takes his seat, oath supervisor takes his seat; (4) Councilors take their seats; (5) Guests take their seats; (6) Sing the Kuomintang song; (7) Bow three times to the Kuomintang flag and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen; (8) Chairman respectfully reads Sun Yat-sen's will; (9) Silent tribute; (10) Chairman delivers the opening address; (11) Councilors take the oath; (12) Oath supervisor delivers an instruction speech; (13) Representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters delivers a speech; (14) Mayor delivers a speech; (15) Guests deliver speeches; (16) Councilors deliver a response speech; (17) Music; (18) Ceremony concludes.

Chairman's Address: Chairman Yu Qiaqing's speech briefly stated: "Today is the day of the inauguration of the Provisional Municipal Council. We are honored to have a representative from the Central Government to supervise the oath, and representatives from various agencies and organizations to participate in the ceremony. We are deeply honored. We hope to receive much guidance in the future. Our city is in a prime location and its situation is different from other provinces and cities. Shanghai is not only a commercial center and a diplomatic center, but also a center of world opinion. Considering the development process of Shanghai, the initial revenue was less than 300,000 taels. In the era of Lu Yongxiang, it was only 700,000. After the establishment of the Municipal Government, due to the rectification and planning of successive mayors, the Municipal treasury revenue has been nearly 10 million. Although some were destroyed by the war this spring, it is still the leading city in the country. We are recommended by the mayor and will do our best to assist the mayor to make all the construction of this city more perfect, comparable to major cities in Europe and the United States."

Oath Supervisor's Address: Chu Minyi's oath supervision speech briefly stated: "Mayor, councilors, guests, today the councilors of the Shanghai Provisional Municipal Council are holding an oath-taking ceremony. I represent the Central Government and the Executive Yuan to supervise the oath, and I feel exceptionally honored and very happy. Shanghai is a major international trading port, and its international reputation is at stake. Its importance surpasses that of all other parts of the country. Unfortunately, since the January 28 Incident, the Jiangwan and Zhabei areas have been completely destroyed by artillery fire. It is extremely painful to mention. In the era of former Mayor Zhang Yuejun, there was already a plan for a Greater Shanghai. Since Mayor Wu took office, he has been working hard to continue the process and will see it implemented in stages. Therefore, I discussed with Mayor Wu and proposed to the Central Government to establish the Shanghai Provisional Municipal Council. The councilors are all outstanding talents of the time and are appointed by the Municipal Government. This is because Shanghai's position is so important and construction is urgent and cannot be delayed. Therefore, it is impossible to manage without collective efforts. Today, the Provisional Municipal Council has been established, and the councilors have taken office. I sincerely hope that they will work hard to serve and directly seek happiness for the citizens of the entire city, and indirectly benefit the country. In the future, after the Greater Shanghai plan is realized, I will celebrate with you all."

Representative's Speech: Pan Gongzhan, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, gave a speech, briefly stating: "I represent the Municipal Party Headquarters to offer a few words. First, all municipal councilors are leaders from all walks of life in this city. Today, they have accepted the invitation of the mayor and the Central Government to take the oath of office here, and they must be very clear about their duties. According to the provisions of the Municipal Organization Law, each city should have a Municipal Council. However, the formal Municipal Council must be produced by election. The Provisional Municipal Council is recommended by the mayor and appointed by the Executive Yuan. Although the name and method of production are different, their powers are the same. The Municipal Party Headquarters believes that the so-called party governance is only a means of the transitional period. The ultimate goal is of course not democratic governance, but to achieve democratic governance from party governance, we must go through various procedures step by step. The Provisional Municipal Council can be said to be the public opinion organ of the transitional period before the formal Municipal Council is produced. As for the powers, they are exactly the same. I sincerely hope that all councilors will exercise the special powers given to them and represent the citizens to contribute suggestions that are beneficial to the citizens to the Municipal Government. Second, some people say that the so-called public opinion organ should be produced by election. Now, the Provisional Municipal Council is established because of the government's appointment. Can it represent public opinion? According to the Municipal Party Headquarters, the so-called public opinion refers to the entire, non-class-based, and clear public opinion, not the meaning of a specific elector. The original intention of the election is nothing more than to trust their personality and knowledge, and they can represent public opinion. This time, the Municipal Government also trusts your knowledge and morality and can represent public opinion, so it is appointed as a councilor. Therefore, its role is no different from that of an elected person. Third, we can trust that you can be competent for this task when we look at your past careers, knowledge, experience, morality, and deeply admire Mayor Wu's vision in selecting and appointing people. At the same time, among you, there are people from the banking industry, industrialists, scholars, journalists, lawyers, accountants, and other self-employed people. Not only do you have the ability and experience, but you are all local leaders who are trusted. Mayor Wu has actually recruited all of you. Therefore, the mayor's selection of councilors can be said to be meticulous. This Provisional Municipal Council will surely represent the entire public opinion. I believe that if the method of voting is used to elect people, it may not be possible to recruit leaders from all walks of life in one place. Furthermore, in recent years, there have been many malpractices in the election system. Since you are invited, your integrity is incomparable to those who are elected through sports elections. I would like to represent the Municipal Party Headquarters to wish you a bright future."

Mayor's Address: "Oath Supervisor, councilors, guests, fellow citizens of Shanghai, the three million citizens have been eagerly hoping for the early establishment of a public opinion organ, so that the reconstruction of Shanghai can be realized as soon as possible and the happiness of the three million citizens can be sought. The Municipal Government colleagues follow the three million citizens and also hope that the public opinion organ can be realized as soon as possible, so that the various policies of this city can be consulted and there can be a guideline. Today, it can actually be realized. This is not only a happy thing for the Municipal Government colleagues, but also a happy thing for the citizens of the entire city. Since the January 28 Incident, most of the construction projects in Shanghai have been destroyed, suffering unprecedented losses. If we want to restore the old appearance and build a more prosperous situation than before, it will not be possible without the concerted efforts of the citizens and the government. As for what method we should use to show that all the citizens and the Municipal Government are working together, only the method of the Municipal Council can express this spirit and convey public opinion. However, the formal Municipal Council must have considerable procedures and a considerable period of time before it can be established. The suffering of the citizens of Shanghai after the war and the urgency of the reconstruction project cannot be delayed until the establishment of this formal Municipal Council. Therefore, for emergency purposes, there is a proposal to the Central Government to establish a Provisional Municipal Council. However, we respect the Provisional Municipal Council as much as the formal Municipal Council. We hope that the councilors will work together with one heart and one mind to assist the Municipal Government colleagues, relieve the people's suffering, and meet the needs of the citizens. I would like to express my sincere respect to the councilors on the day of the establishment of the Provisional Municipal Council."

Guest Speech: Lin Kanghou, representative of the guests, gave a speech: "The establishment of the Provisional Municipal Council today fully demonstrates the cooperation between the Municipal Government and the citizens. From now on, all public opinions can be conveyed by this council to the Municipal Government. I would like to represent the citizens to congratulate Mayor Wu and the councilors on the successful cooperation and the early realization of Greater Shanghai, and the early elimination of the suffering of the citizens. At the same time, I would like to quote a few sentences from the Four Books as a contribution. The Four Books say, 'Those who produce are many, those who consume are few, those who work are quick, and those who use are thrifty, then wealth will always be sufficient.' I deeply feel that if we want to make the city prosperous, the first thing we must do is to make everyone have a job. The so-called 'those who produce are many' is right. The excessive taxes and miscellaneous levies on the people should be reduced as much as possible. This is the so-called 'those who consume are few' is right. 'Those who work are quick, and those who use are thrifty' means that finance should be based on income and expenditure. The result of the economic panic in European and American countries is to abandon the policy of basing expenditure on income and instead create a system of basing expenditure on income, which leads to financial difficulties and heavy taxes on the people. This is not the way to govern. I hope that the Municipal Council will follow this principle in the future and cooperate with the Municipal Government at any time. Even if there are things that want to increase the burden on the people, please make it public so that the citizens know the ins and outs of the municipal administration. If everything can be made public, so as to achieve the effect of cooperation between the government and the people, then the future will be really reliable."

Councilor's Response: The Municipal Councilors' representative responded, "I have just heard the instructions from the oath supervisor, the mayor, and the guests. We are very admirable and will definitely encourage ourselves in the future to cooperate with the mayor to achieve the completion of the construction of Greater Shanghai. On behalf of all the councilors, I would like to thank you all."

Holding a Consultation Meeting: After the Municipal Councilors finished their response, the ceremony was completed in the melodious sound of music, followed by refreshments and photography. After the photography, all the councilors gathered in the conference room on the left side of the Foreign Affairs Building to convene the first consultation meeting. It was decided to convene a formal meeting next week to elect the speaker, etc.

Discussing Ways to Maximize Loans Secured by Grain

Leaders from All Walks of Life Raise Several Points

Financial Minister Song Ziwen, in view of the severe drop in rice prices and the impending bankruptcy of the rural economy, was eager to find ways to provide relief. Communist Leader Chen Duxiu and Others Arrested 129

Broken After Two Days and Nights of Searching

Chen and Eleven Others All Sent to the Public Security Bureau

Among the Communists, there is a so-called Trotskyist faction, which organized the Youth League Committee in Shanghai, electing five committee members to handle party affairs. Chen Duxiu is the leader of this group, giving instructions and commands. The party members all follow his lead. The committee stipulated that a standing meeting should be held once a week. Recently, Chen, due to his weak health, has been represented by Xie Shaoshan in every meeting and guidance work. The authorities, considering that the party is engaged in the exclusive dissemination of communist propaganda and that Du Xiu has long been wanted by the government, strictly ordered the police to secretly investigate and arrest them to curb the chaos. Recently, the Municipal Public Security Bureau discovered that Chen and important members of the party were hiding in various places in the Public Concession and the French Concession. The Bureau Chief Wen Hongen consulted the First Special District Local Court and issued search warrants and arrest warrants, dispatching detectives from the political department of the General Inspectorate and Chinese and Western detectives from the Jiaxing Road Police Station to start operations at 2:30 PM on the 15th (last Saturday). After two days and nights, until the night of the 16th, all the famous figures of the party were captured. The seized communist propaganda documents and books were too numerous to be counted. It can be said to be the first major case since the purge of the Communists. The destruction of various agencies and the interrogation situation are described below:

Five People Arrested in Chunyangli: At 2:30 PM last Saturday, Chinese and Western detectives, with court search warrants and arrest warrants, first went to No. 210 Chunyangli, Dongyouheng Road, and arrested five people: Xie Shaoshan (22 years old) from Guangdong, Wang Zhaoqun (27 years old) from Anhui, Zhang Cinan (34 years old) from Hunan, Pu Yifan (28 years old) from Anhui, and Wang Wu (35 years old) from Hebei. 106 documents and 34 kinds of Russian communist books were seized and taken back to the Jiaxing Road Police Station for detention. Among these five people, Zhang Cinan's original name was Peng Shuzhi, and it was heard that Xie Shaoshan's other name was Xie Depei.

Chen Duxiu's Appearance: After the search in Chunyangli, they went to No. 11 Yongjili, Yuezhou Road, to search. Chen Duxiu was alone in the room. The detectives immediately arrested him and seized many communist documents in Chinese, Japanese, and Russian in his room. Chen was also taken to the police station. Chen is from Anhui, 54 years old this year. He is very thin due to illness, with a slight beard on his lips and slightly gray hair. He was wearing a light blue serge long gown and a light yellow felt hat. After being detained in the police station, the head of the police inquired about his illness and sent a detective to the Public Works Department hospital. The doctor diagnosed that his illness was not very serious and that he could be interrogated.

Searching Pu's Residence: After Pu Yifan, Secretary-General and Translator of China Merchants Avoiding Secrets, was arrested in Chunyangli, the police station found out that he lived at No. 222 Gaofuli, Avenue Notre Dame, French Concession. The detectives rushed to the French police station to request assistance and went to Pu's home with the French detectives to search. More than 30 kinds of communist documents were found and taken back to the police station.

Western Police Jumping Out of Windows to Chase: At 11:00 PM on the 15th, Chinese and Western detectives secretly went to No. 1044 Siwenli, Xinzha Grand Avenue, to ambush the remaining party members. A Guangxi person, Liang Youguang, was arrested. Two others jumped out of the window of their room to escape. A Western policeman from a certain house also jumped out of the window to chase and eventually caught Wang Xiaochun (30 years old) from Anhui. The other person escaped without a trace. 28 documents were seized in the room and Liang and Wang were taken back to the police station for strict detention.

Continuing the Search the Next Day: Police station detectives continued to work the next day from morning to evening. First, they went to No. 335 Yeguangli, Tangshan Road, and arrested Wang Ziping and He Afang, two people from Wenzhou. 78 kinds of Russian documents were seized. Then, they went to No. 22 Jianyeli, Fuxuli Road, French Concession, and arrested Wang Jiantang, a person from Shandong. 10 documents and books and a piece of carbon paper were seized. The paper had only been used once, and the handwriting was still recognizable, all of which were communist propaganda words. Then, they went to No. 532 Xiudeli, Baker Road, to search. The person living in the house had already fled after hearing the news, leaving a note in the room. The words written were to notify the party members that the agency in a certain place had been destroyed and not to go there again. In addition, eight documents were also seized. There were also three places where the gangs had been: No. 284 Avenue Joffre, No. 3 Shanjili, East Jiaxing Road, and a certain number of Baker Road No. 394 Lane. When they went to search, they had all escaped in advance and left nothing behind. Therefore, there was nothing to be found in these three places.

Indictment of Defendants: Yesterday morning, the police station escorted Chen Duxiu and the other eleven people who had been arrested one after another to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Various documents and books were also transported to the court by car. Judge Zhao Zhengcheng then took the seat in the First Tribunal to propose the case. In order to make it easier for the court to understand the case, the police station attached numbers to the chests of each defendant. For example, Chen Duxiu was No. 6 when he was arrested, so he was attached with the number 6 as the sixth defendant. Because Chen was ill, he was allowed to sit. The police station lawyer Li Zhishan described the process of solving the case and said that the indictment was based on Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the Emergency Law on Punishing Acts Endangering the Republic of China and Article 6 of the same law.

Page 14

Defendant Chen Duxiu had been punished by the former French Concession police twice in the French Concession in the 11th and 13th years of the Republic of China for propagating Bolshevism, with a fine of 100 yuan for the first time and 400 yuan for the second time. Wang Zhaoqun had been punished in the 18th year for a case. Wang Wu had also been arrested and sent to the Garrison Headquarters for interrogation in a communist case. Now, it is still necessary to investigate and request a change of date.

Public Security Bureau Requests Transfer: The representative of the Municipal Public Security Bureau went to court and said, "Chen Duxiu, one of the defendants in this case, is an important criminal wanted by the government. Whether the police station prosecutes this person or not, they must be allowed to be transferred to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation and handling, because all the major cases he committed were in the mainland and he lived in the concession, relying on it as a talisman. Xie Shaoshan is also requested to be transferred to the bureau for interrogation and then sent back to your court, and it is requested to prohibit spectators from attending." The police station lawyer declared that they did not object to the temporary transfer of Xie Shaoshan to the bureau for interrogation.

Secret Interrogation of Defendants: Judge Zhao, considering that the confessions of the defendants were extremely important in this case and could not be leaked, immediately announced a ban on spectators and ordered all the defendants to be taken to the waiting room for separate interrogation. It was not over by noon, so he ordered Xie Shaoshan to be handed over to the Public Security Bureau personnel to take away first.

The Police Station Withdraws the Prosecution: At 2:00 PM, Judge Zhao opened the First Tribunal again to continue the separate interrogation. First, Li Zhishan of the police station declared that, after investigation, it had been found that some of the defendants had not committed all the crimes in the concession. For the convenience of investigation and interrogation, the police station requested permission to withdraw the prosecution. The police station did not object to the transfer of all defendants as requested by the Municipal Public Security Bureau.

Public Security Bureau Requests Transfer: The lawyer representing the Public Security Bureau solemnly declared again that many of the defendants had been wanted by the government. Now that the police station has requested to withdraw the prosecution, they should be transferred to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation and handling in accordance with the agreement. Judge Zhao then interrogated each of the defendants who had not been interrogated one by one. It was exactly 4:30, so he temporarily retired from the court.

Ruling Granting Transfer: At 5:00, Criminal Tribunal President Yu Hua, Judge Zhao Zhengcheng, and Guo Huaipu, together with the prosecutor, convened a conference court. After the police station lawyer and the Public Security Bureau lawyer sequentially stated the course of events, the prosecutor then stood up and argued that since the police station had withdrawn the prosecution, the Public Security Bureau should take them away in accordance with the agreement. President Yu declared that Chen Duxiu and the other eleven people would be handed over to the personnel from the Municipal Public Security Bureau to take away for interrogation and handling.

Defendants Express Opinions: The defendants stood up and protested after hearing the ruling. Wang Xiaochun, Pu Yifan, and Liang Youguang spoke the most. Chen Duxiu only spoke a few words, but it can be said to be concise and comprehensive. What they argued was all legal issues, expressing their unwillingness to have the case transferred to the Public Security Bureau. President Yu earnestly instructed that this transfer procedure was handled in accordance with the agreement, and even if an appeal was made, it could not stop the execution of this ruling. The defendants continued to argue, speaking one after another, which took a long time. The court thought that it was a waste of time and effort, and it was difficult to expect them to understand. Therefore, when the clock struck six, the court was adjourned, and the personnel from the Public Security Bureau escorted the defendants, along with the seized documents and books, into cars and took them to the bureau for interrogation and handling.

Righteous Army Support Association 133

Soliciting Material Objects to Aid the Righteous Army

Seventeen Categories of Cloth and Other Items

And Marketable Items

Money is Solicited at the Same Time

The Shanghai Northern Righteous Army Support Association believes that if it only raises cash to aid the Righteous Army, the amount obtained will be difficult to meet the demand. Moreover, at this time of national economic exhaustion, it is especially difficult to make ends meet. The directors of the association have repeatedly planned ways to increase the amount of donations, and feel that the amount cannot be increased unless money and goods are collected and solicited at the same time. Therefore, they have passed the [Regulations for the Handling of Solicited Material Objects] in fifteen articles at the 62nd executive committee meeting. There are seventeen items of solicited material objects. The original text is recorded as follows: (Chapter 1) General Principles (Article 1) In order to increase fundraising efficiency, this association will solicit material objects at the same time as soliciting money. (Article 2) The types of material objects solicited by this association are as follows: (1) Cloth, (2) Cotton, (3) Silk Cotton, (4) Cotton Clothes, (5) Leather Clothes, (6) Leather Materials, (7) Medicines, (8) Food, (9) Medical Equipment, (10) Transportation Equipment, (11) Telescopes and Goggles, (12) Tents, (13) Engineering Tools, (14) Manufacturing Parts, (15) Paintings by Famous Artists, (16) Jewelry and Treasures, (17) All Marketable Items. Article 3) This Association

The material objects obtained by this association that are suitable for use in front of the army will be directly delivered to the various righteous armies for use. The marketable items will be converted into money and allocated to the various armies. (Article 4) This association will organize a price conversion committee to handle the marketable items obtained. Article 5: This association will establish a receiving and management office and a storage office, all of which are under the command and supervision of the standing directors, and will be responsible for their duties. (Chapter 2) Collection and Storage (Article 6) In addition to direct receipt, this association will entrust legal organizations with good reputation to be responsible for collection on its behalf. (Article 7) All donors of material objects, whether directly delivered to this association or to the collection points, will be verified by the receiving personnel on the spot for the name, quality, texture, and quantity of the items, and the intended use and value will be clearly stated. A formal receipt will be filled out according to the format and handed over to the donor for safekeeping. (Article 8) For those directly received by this association, the receiving office shall fill out a notice form according to the format and hand it over to the management office together with the material objects for inspection and acceptance, and enter it into the account according to the number, and take the inspection and acceptance voucher as proof. (Article 9) For the items received by the collection points, the receiving personnel shall fill out a notice form according to the format and send it to the association, and then the management office of this association shall send personnel to inspect and enter it into the account, and issue a voucher as proof. (Article 10) The items inspected and accepted by the management office shall be issued with a storage ticket on the same day and sent to the storage office for verification and registration for safekeeping. (Article 11) The storage office may borrow warehouses and vaults for storing items. (Article 12) The management office shall list the income and stored items daily and submit them to the standing director committee, the custody committee, and the supervisory committee for record. (Chapter 3 Issuance (Article 13) All items decided by the standing director committee to be issued to the various armies for use, or to be converted into money, shall be checked by the management office, and a request form, notification form, and bill of lading shall be filled out, submitted to the standing director committee for approval, and then forwarded to the custody committee for signature, and then forwarded to the supervisory committee for verification. If there is no difference, it shall be returned to the standing director committee for countersignature, and the bill of lading shall be handed over to the recipient to extract the items from the storage office. (Chapter 4) Account Books and Vouchers (Article 14) The account books and vouchers used by this association for soliciting material objects are as follows: (1) The receiving office and the collection points do not establish account books, and each uses the receipt stub as proof (2) The management office sets up a fundraising account, listing the number, and recording the month, day, name, quality, texture, quantity, use, value, storage location, receiving location, and notification number 3 The storage office sets up a storage account, listing the number, recording the month, day, name, quantity, and fundraising account number. After the items are issued, it also records the month, day, and bill of lading number of the extraction (4 The storage office receives the items recorded in the storage ticket, and after recording the account number, it shall fill in the account number in the receipt and return it to the management office (5) The management office establishes a separate account, uniformly recording the order, type, and breadth of receipt by each household (Article 15) These regulations shall be implemented from the date of approval by the council, and any matters not covered shall be proposed for amendment by the standing director council

It is also heard that the locations for collecting material objects of the association, in addition to the association's office, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on Tianhougong Bridge and the Lawyers Association at the intersection of Lafayette Road and Beile Road, have all agreed to receive them on behalf of the association.

Local News Two

Chopping at the Copper of a Bomb 138

Woman on the Verge of Death

Two Children Also Seriously Injured

After the January 28th Incident, a large number of cannons and bombs were left in the fields and streams in the northern suburbs of Shanghai, especially around Wusong Township. Ignorant villagers are often harmed. Yang, a local resident of Liujiazhai, west of Wusong Township, whose son, Xing Sheng, is 18 years old, went with his nephew, Gen Da (7 years old, to a nearby stream for a cold bath in mid-June of this summer. Not long after entering the water, they discovered a heavy object at the bottom of the bank, an 80-pound bomb. They carried it home and placed it indoors for four months. His mother, Gu, caught a glimpse of the heavy copper on both ends of the bomb, which was very valuable, and had long been coveting it. At 7:00 a.m. yesterday, she and her son, Xing Sheng, and nephew, Gen Da, held iron axes and struck at both ends of the bomb. Before long, there was a loud bang, and the bomb exploded. Gu was injured in her limbs, and her life could not be saved. She is on the verge of death. Xing Sheng was injured in his abdomen, and his fingers were completely destroyed. Only Gen Da was slightly injured. They were sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment by car.

Yesterday's Memorial Service for Zhang Jinlong Zhang Jinlong, a squad leader of the Shanghai South District Defense Corps in this city, bravely went out to defend against the Japanese during the Anti-Japanese War, overworked himself, and died. Mr. Ma Xiangbo, Dai Ji, and others initiated a memorial meeting, which has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday, a memorial service was held at the headquarters of the Eighth Team, presided over by Vice Minister Zhao Jinqing. More than 200 guests attended, including Qu Wenliu, Chairman Zhang Bingxin, Yu Baoqing, and Zhu Shaoyi. At the ceremony, Huang Ruisheng, chairman of the association, reported the purpose, and Feng Runsheng, the team leader, announced Zhang Jinlong's deeds and respectfully read the memorial text. In addition, Vice Minister Zhao delivered a speech, saying that after the Northeast Incident, Zhang Jinlong joined the Defense Corps to do his best for the country. Those who cherish their lives would not do that. Therefore, his loyalty and courage are admirable, and his talent is naturally useful to the country. His death is very regrettable. Then, Chief Director Qu Wenliu delivered a speech, saying, "What is the reason for our memorial service for Mr. Zhang? Mr. Zhang died in the rear defense. When the whole country is fighting desperately against Japan, there is only the distinction of pointing the gun outwards. How can there be a reason for attacking the rear when the front line is fighting? This is a strange phenomenon that does not exist in other countries in the world. Therefore, Mr. Zhang's death in the rear is not worth it. We mourn Mr. Zhang and should sigh for the country." Finally, Zhu Shaoyi, Zhang Bingxin, Gu Zhujun, and others successively gave speeches. The meeting adjourned after 7 p.m.

Record of the Autumn General Meeting of the Doctors' Association The Shanghai Doctors' Association held its autumn general meeting on the 16th at Yipinxiang on Xizang Road. More than 200 members attended, including Song Guobin, Chu Minyi, Yu Yunzhen, Long Jingzhou, Wang Qizhang, Xu Naili, and Cai Yumen. The meeting was chaired by Song Guobin and others, recorded by Cheng Hanzhang, and hosted by Jiang Zhenxun. The proceedings of the meeting were reported in yesterday's newspaper. The following is a record of the important motions discussed and resolved on that day, as well as a list of the elected executive and supervisory committee members: (1) Discussion on the method of flexibly issuing doctor's certificates. It was resolved that the National Doctors' Federation should be requested to submit a petition to the central government to handle the matter according to the original policy. (2) Formulation of the association's current consultation fee regulations. It was resolved that the principle be approved and that a committee be formed to revise the regulations, with Song Guobin, Zhu Yanggao, Pang Jingzhou, Wu Yichu, Wang Wanbai, Xu Jihua, Cai Shicun, and Xu Naili being nominated as members. (3) How should the association's personnel participating in national crisis work be rewarded? It was resolved that it be publicized in the yearbook for remembrance. (4) Amendment of Articles 3, 4, 5, and 8 of the association's articles of association. It was resolved that the amendments be made according to the proposal of the Standing Committee, and that Wang Qizhang be responsible for organizing the passage. (5) How should those who contributed to the regular expenses of the National General Association of New Medicine be rewarded? It was resolved that the new executive committee be tasked with finding a way to handle it. (6) Discussion on the plan to assist the Northeast Volunteer Army. It was resolved that the association should advance 3,000 yuan and request that all members share the cost equally. (7) It was resolved that pharmaceutical merchants should submit the drugs they promote to the association for review before distributing them to the members. The association should initiate a joint committee with the National Doctors' Federation and other organizations to handle the matter. (8) If a doctor has his own pharmacy, the prescriptions used should be given to the patient and not taken back for reference by other doctors during diagnosis. It was resolved that it be approved. (9) It was proposed that the association build a complete hospital. It was resolved that it be withdrawn. Temporary proposals are as follows: (1) It was resolved that members of the association should display a sign to make themselves known to the public. (2) It was resolved that the association should prepare a relief project to fulfill its duties. Distribution vouchers should be issued by district, with the names of doctors in the district listed. (3) It was resolved that enemy goods should be strictly boycotted, and active measures should be taken to promote the Japanese medicine reference list, which should be distributed to doctors nationwide by the National Doctors' Federation. (4) It was resolved that the method of taking prescriptions should be unified to ensure the accuracy of the medicine. Future prescriptions should specify (how many grids, one grid per dose, how many days to take). (5) It was resolved that hospitals and clinics should no longer be allowed to hire male nurses in the future. It was resolved that nurses should be women in principle in order to promote women's careers. (6) Proceed with the registration of the association. It was resolved that the association is a local organization and has been approved for registration by the municipal party and government organs, so the original proposal was withdrawn. (7) It was resolved that the association should request the National Doctors' Federation to submit a petition to amend the government's crackdown on informal medical groups. It was resolved that it be reserved. After the discussion, the officers were re-elected. As a result, Wang Qizhang, Pang Jingzhou, Yu Yunxiu, Cai Yumen, Xia Shenchu, Xu Naili, Ye Zhisheng, Zhu Qiluo, Zhu Yanggao, Liu Zhigang, Xie Yunshou, Wu Yichu, Niu Huisheng, Jin Wenqi, and Cheng Hanzhang were elected as executive committee members. Song Guobin, Jiang Zhenxun, You Pengxi, Chu Minyi, and Tang Shouxian were elected as supervisory committee members.

Lida Academy Farm Opens Chicken Farming Practice Class Lida Academy in Jiangwan, this city, has been promoting production education for many years. It has established a farm in Jiangwan and a rural education department in Chaitang, Nanxiang, both of which have achieved remarkable results. This year, when the violent Japanese invaded, all the products and equipment of the academy's farm and all the production bases of the rural education department were almost completely destroyed. However, more than 2,000 fine breeding chickens raised on the farm were fortunately moved out by a quarter under the rain of bullets and transported to Wuxi, Jiaxing, and other places to be preserved. After the Japanese invaders withdrew, the academy worked hard to restore the farm, which is now焕然一新. Although the original chicken farm area has been slightly reduced due to the reduction in the number of chickens, there are still more than 500 fine breeding chickens that can be developed. At present, all parties feel that it is necessary to study, improve, and promote the chicken farming industry, and many people have requested to practice at the farm. In response to the needs of the situation, the farm has decided to open a chicken farming practice class to enable those interested in chicken farming to conduct practical research on the farm, which will surely greatly benefit the future rural economy.

Hongkou Nanlu Request to Exempt Municipal Donations Unsuccessful Taxpayers Association Sends Letter to Public Works Bureau Yesterday The letter stated: In response to your letter of October 4, since the 28th, the authorities of the concession, in view of the difficulties of the people in the area, have reduced and exempted the spring municipal donations to regulate people's livelihoods. The law is very good. Our factory is located in the eastern district, adjacent to the trenches. The degree of disaster is deeper than other places. At that time, the rent problem had not been resolved, and there was no corresponding standard, so we temporarily paid one month of spring municipal donations to fulfill our tax obligations. Now that the rent dispute has been resolved and two months have been waived, we believe that the collection of municipal donations is purely based on rent. By analogy, the Public Works Bureau should also waive three months on this basis. Moreover, there is a precedent in Nanlufang, dozens of steps away from our factory. Therefore, we send this letter to your association and ask for your assistance, and hope that you will send a letter to the Public Works Bureau, requesting them to return the overcharged one month of spring municipal donations to alleviate the people's difficulties. After investigation, the Public Works Bureau of the Public Concession exempted the municipal donations in the Hongkou area for a maximum of three months and a minimum of one and a half months. The decision was made after careful consideration and negotiation. The original intention was to save the market, and there is no causal relationship between the exemption of rent or not. Moreover, the budget of the Public Works Bureau has a certain amount. This time, the general exemption of the municipal donations in the Hongkou area is a huge amount. Our association once asked for more exemption, but the answer was that reducing the burden of taxpayers in the Hongkou area would inevitably increase the burden of other taxpayers, which is very unfair. Our association cannot be biased towards taxpayers, so we also agree with this statement. There is another thing that can be told, that is, the owner, for the sake of rent exemption, once asked the Public Works Bureau to exempt land donations, but it was not approved. This situation should not be ignored. The above is the reason for the letter, and the attachments are enclosed for your reference.

In order to satisfy the guests, the association has spent a lot of money to hire the great European orchestra to play various famous songs of the era, and so on.

Achievements of Acupuncture Expert Ma Maoqing Acupuncture expert Ma Maoqing used to practice medicine in Zhenjiang for more than 30 years and cured many serious illnesses. After coming to Shanghai, he set up a clinic at Jingqinfang, Zhejiang Road, and a branch clinic at Taihe Street in the alley opposite the Rui Rong Factory in Yangshupu.

Bei Hai Opera Troupe Rehearses Today The Shanghai Bei Hai Opera Troupe has been well-known since its establishment. After the first rehearsal, the members have become more enthusiastic and the internal research has been strengthened. It is now scheduled to hold the second rehearsal at the Ningbo Tongxiang Hall on Xizang Road at 6 p.m. today. At that time, the drums and music will be loud and there will be a grand occasion.

Fire on Gordon Road This Morning At 0:03 this morning, the Biju Art Woodware Company at No. 132 Gordon Road was careless, and suddenly thick smoke billowed and the fire was bright. One building was burned down. After the fire brigade rushed to help, it was extinguished after more than an hour.

Salt Affairs Auditing Office Colleagues 142

Actively Assist the Northeast Volunteer Army

Two Thousand Yuan Remitted by the Bank of China

The colleagues of the Salt Affairs Auditing Office of the Ministry of Finance, with their patriotic enthusiasm, have always been second to none. Previously, during the 19th Route Army's anti-Japanese operations in Shanghai, the colleagues of the general and branch offices generously donated funds totaling more than two thousand yuan. Now, the colleagues of the general office, considering that the Northeast has been lost for a year, and our thirty million compatriots are being trampled upon by foreign invaders, living in dire straits and suffering the pain of national subjugation, are fortunate that the loyal and brave volunteer army of the three provinces is shedding blood on the battlefield, making continuous efforts to cause the brutal Japanese warlords to flee in panic and suffer heavy losses. The glorious battle achievements are frequently seen in the newspapers. It is said that the volunteer army is short of weapons, clothing, medical supplies, and other necessities, and is in a very difficult situation. Without assistance, how can they survive? Considering that every citizen is responsible for the rise and fall of the nation, and the anti-Japanese war in the Northeast cannot achieve success in a short period, the best way to donate funds is to make monthly subscriptions for long-term assistance. Currently, two thousand yuan has been raised and sent to the Bank of China for remittance. In the future, monthly payments of approximately the same amount will be made. Various auditing branch offices are also initiating similar efforts. Other organizations, groups, and merchants are said to be responding to the call with sympathy.

Companies and Firms in the Same Trade Should All Be Members of the Trade Association 143

Explicitly Promulgated by the National Government

The Social Affairs Bureau yesterday instructed the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating, "For your information, as per the Municipal Government's instruction No. 2890, which states, 'As per the Executive Yuan's instruction No. 3893, which states, "As per the National Government's Luo Zi instruction No. 238, after investigation, the Trade Association Law of Industry and Commerce has been formulated and explicitly promulgated. Now, Article 7 of the said law has been slightly amended and should be immediately implemented. In addition to separate orders, a copy of the amended article is sent for your information and to instruct your subordinates to be informed accordingly," etc., based on this, in addition to separate orders, a copy of the amended article is sent for your information and to instruct your subordinate trade associations to be informed accordingly. This order includes the following amended articles of the Trade Association Law: Article 7: Companies and firms in the same trade should all be members of the trade association and send representatives to attend the association, but those who have been expelled are not subject to this restriction."'"

Shanghai-Chongming-Ningbo-Zhoushan Ferry Damaged Machinery 144

Tianci Towed into Wusong

Passengers and Cargo All Safe

The Shanghai-Chongming-Ningbo-Zhoushan ferry, the Yongzhou, departed from Nanmengang Port in Chongming at 7:00 yesterday morning. After passing Qixiao and other places in Zhen, it arrived at the Sanchashui sea area outside Wusongkou at around 11:00. Suddenly, in the engine room, a screw on the engine's starter was broken and fell off due to the force of the waves, causing the entire machine to malfunction and stop automatically. After the incident, the chief engineer immediately reported to the shipowner, who dropped anchor at the site. At that time, the Tianci, a ship on the same route from Shanghai to Chongming, was returning. The shipowner immediately pulled the whistle and waved the flag. After the Tianci saw this, it sailed closer to the Yongzhou. The Yongzhou shipowner explained the damaged machinery and asked the Tianci to tow it back to Shanghai. The Tianci shipowner agreed and immediately towed the Yongzhou with a cable. When towing into Wusongkou, the Jiuru tugboat, which was returning from towing oil tankers in Baozhen, saw the Yongzhou being towed by the Tianci and voluntarily offered to tow it to Shanghai. Therefore, the Yongzhou was towed into Wusongkou by the Jiuru tugboat, while the Tianci turned around and headed to Chongming. The Yongzhou arrived in Shanghai at around 3:00 and docked at Pier No. 9 in the South City. Passengers and cargo were all safe. It was originally scheduled to depart for Chongming today, but due to machinery repairs, one voyage has been temporarily suspended and is expected to resume as usual the day after tomorrow.

Minutes of the Shanghai County Government Meeting 145

This Year's Second Term Land Price Tax Begins

Collection of Party Affairs Fees of Three Cents Per Mu

The Shanghai County Government held its 123rd county government meeting at 10:00 AM yesterday. The attendees included the heads of the Finance, Construction, and Education Bureaus, the director of property, the secretary of the county government, the section chiefs, and Chairman Yan Shenyu (Secretary Ye Dehuan acting on his behalf). Hu Gongshou recorded the meeting. The meeting began as scheduled, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) The county magistrate submitted a proposal based on the results of the Party and Government Talks to request the collection of party affairs expenses of three cents per mu, starting from the second term land price tax this year. The proposal was approved. (2) The county magistrate submitted a proposal based on an order from the Provincial Land Bureau urging the organization of a land survey and custody committee to comply with the order. The proposal resolved that the county land bureau and the county chamber of commerce committee should submit a report to the provincial bureau for instructions and then comply. (3) The county magistrate submitted a proposal based on an order from the Construction Department to collect construction special donations from tooth tax, which should be based on the highest amount actually collected in the past three years as a fixed amount, with 5% of the donation used as expenses. How should other surtaxes be handled? The proposal resolved that the county will collect various surcharges in accordance with the standards stipulated by the Construction Department. The highest amount actually collected in the past three years will be investigated and replied by the Finance Bureau, and merchants will be ordered to pay according to the certificate. (4) The County Construction Bureau proposed whether public bicycles can be exempted from donations. It was resolved that vehicle donations may be appropriately exempted.

Residents of Western Shanghai Urge Dredging of the Pu Zhao River 146

Bringing Two Bottles of Sewage

Together to the Municipal Government to Petition

The Pu Zhao River in Western Shanghai has not been dredged for many years. The silt is shallow and dirty, affecting irrigation, transportation, and residents' drinking water. Ma Xiangbo and others jointly submitted a request to the municipal government to plan dredging. More than a month has passed, and no instructions have been received. The public is eagerly waiting, like clouds and rain. Yesterday, it was reported that more than 50 representatives of the people of Shangqingsong Sanjie in Western Shanghai, including Ma Xiangbo (representative), Yang Xinzheng, Zhang Weicheng, Gu Xiaoqing, Chen Ya'fu, Li Qixian, Shen Caigeng, Li Youxian, Gu Houjie, Xia Rusheng, Wang Jingzhi, Wang Daoxing, Li Wenlai, Pan Boxian, and Tang Zu, brought two bottles of sewage from the river and requested a chemical test and went to the Municipal Government to petition. They were received by Secretary Huang, who first heard the representatives explain that the river water was dirty and shallow, which hindered people's livelihood, and therefore requested that dredging be carried out as soon as possible. Mr. Huang believed that the river definitely needed to be dredged, and the matters presented would be forwarded to the mayor for prompt planning and dredging. The representatives were satisfied and left.

The Two New Ships Funing and Suining 147

Groundbreaking Ceremony Held Yesterday

Wang Shouting Personally Nailed the First Rivet

The Navy Department's two newly built ships, Funing and Suining (formerly planned to be named Anning and Baoning), held a keel-laying ceremony at 9:00 AM yesterday. Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan, due to official duties in Beijing, specially telegraphed Torpedo Commander Wang Shouting to represent him in nailing the first rivet. The details are recorded below:

Attendees: In addition to Torpedo Guerrilla Commander Wang Shouting, those who attended yesterday included Deputy Minister of the Ministry, Chief Supervisor Li Shijia, Deputy Director of the Shipbuilding Plant Chen Zaofan, Guard Battalion Commander Ye Baoqi, Jiangzhen Captain Chen Shaoji, Accounting Section Chief Pan Yingzhou, Bookkeeping Section Chief Chen Zhushen, Machinery Department Chief Zeng Yijing, Supervisors Zeng Guosheng, Huang Yiyan, Shipbuilding Section Director Ye Zaifu, and more than 200 soldiers from the Navy Guard Battalion Jiangzhen Chu with the two ships.

Keel-Laying Situation: Minister Chen, due to official duties in Beijing, specially telegraphed Commander Wang Shouting to represent him in nailing the first rivet. At 9:20, Mr. Tu used force to nail the first rivet that had been burned onto the keel of the Funing ship. It took about five minutes to complete. Then he went to the keel of the Suining ship, where Mr. Wang nailed the first rivet in the same way. The ceremony was completed at 9:30, and Mr. Wang and others dispersed.

Telegram Report: After the keel-laying was completed, the Deputy Director of the Shipbuilding Plant, Chen Zaofan, telegraphed Minister Chen, stating, "To Minister Chen: The keels of the Funing and Suining were laid at 9:00 AM this month, and Commander Wang of the Torpedo Team nailed the first rivet. Sincerely reported, Zaofan kowtows."

Mr. Zeng's Remarks: After the keel-laying, according to Supervisor Zeng Guosheng, who spoke to the Huadong News Agency reporter, the two ships are equivalent to the Jiangning and Haining ships and are specially used for attacking and suppressing river and sea bandits. They are 128 feet long, 20 feet wide, 7 feet draft, 10 nautical miles per hour, 180 tons displacement, and the cost, including armament, is about 250,000 yuan per ship. They are scheduled to be launched in February next year.

Wu Zhongxin Represents the Disaster Situation in Anhui 148

A Wasteland with Boundary Markers Removed, Difficult to Restore

Provincial Government's Financial Resources Exhausted, Unable to Share with Disaster Areas

Mr. Xu Ping, the representative sent by Anhui Provincial Government Chairman Wu Zhongxin to beg for disaster relief, told reporters yesterday that the counties of Liu'an, Yingshan, Tingqiu, and Huoshan in Anhui have fallen into the hands of the Red Bandits for quite some time. Many people have assimilated with the bandits. If relief is not sought urgently, it will be difficult to avoid the old and weak filling the ditches and the strong taking risks. The consequences are unimaginable. The four counties have now become a wasteland, barren and without a grain of harvest. The boundaries of the sea are indistinguishable, and the boundary markers have been removed, making it difficult to reorganize. Recovery is more difficult than last year's flood, and the severity is more than tenfold. Moreover, outside the four counties, in the areas affected by the bandits, there are also Tongcheng, Shucheng, Yingshang, Shou County, Hefei, Susong, Taihu, and Lujiang counties. Although not all of them have been disturbed, the disaster situation is quite serious. For example, the magistrate of Tongcheng County has been taken away by the bandits and is rumored to have been killed. As for the provincial government, its own administrative expenses are still difficult to maintain. Since the reorganization and establishment of the new provincial government five or six months ago, salaries have only been issued for one and a half months, so there is absolutely no surplus to share with the disaster areas. After the representatives came to Shanghai, they contacted various parties. The Anhui Fellow Villagers Association has promised to do its best to find a solution. The Shanghai Provisional Relief Association for Henan and Anhui Disaster Areas held a meeting once yesterday to discuss fundraising methods. The Engineering Department of the National Economic Commission, formerly the Chief Engineer Xi Mingjiu of the Engineering and Relief Department of the National Government's Disaster Relief Association, also promised to find ways to provide engineering relief in the disaster area. However, the survivors are exposed to the elements, with empty stomachs and shivering in the cold wind, and the number of starving people is increasing day by day. This situation is unbearable to describe. I hope that kind-hearted people from all walks of life will show compassion and save our helpless compatriots as soon as possible. On behalf of the provincial government and the disaster victims, I bow and report with sincerity.
